# 如果你成为霸道总裁文里的恶毒女配怎么办？
- 点赞数：14560
- 更新时间：2024年03月11日19时48分03秒
- 回答url：https://www.zhihu.com/question/351039999/answer/927771712
<body>
 <p>我是一个霸道总裁文里的女配<span><span>，</span></span>没错<span><span>，</span></span>就是那种很恶毒的女配<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>你知道我现在在哪吗<span><span>？</span></span>你一定猜不到<span><span>，</span></span>我现在在监狱<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>是的<span><span>，</span></span>这是男主的手笔<span><span>，</span></span>因为我前不久安排了女主的车祸<span><span>，</span></span>据说女主现在还在医院<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>当然<span><span>，</span></span>那可是女主<span><span>，</span></span>怎么可能这么轻易死去<span><span>？</span></span>遭殃的还是我<span><span>，</span></span>我被男主送进了监狱<span><span>，</span></span>以<span><span>「</span></span>故意伤害罪<span><span>」</span></span><span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>呵<span><span>，</span></span>进监狱就进监狱吧<span><span>，</span></span>我可是官方认定的<span><span>，</span></span>身家背景<span><span>、</span></span>学历相貌都和男主相匹配的恶毒女配<span><span>，</span></span>作为这么一个优秀女配<span><span>，</span></span>我的家族自然不会让我在监狱受苦<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>2776 出来<span><span>，</span></span>家人保释<span><span>，</span></span>你可以出去了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>狱警用警棍敲了敲监狱房间的门<span><span>，</span></span>我缓缓从床上坐起来<span><span>。</span></span>这是我意料之中的结果<span><span>，</span></span>以我的家世背景<span><span>，</span></span>我父母自然不会允许他们的女儿有坐过牢的经历<span><span>，</span></span>无论他们的女儿犯了什么大错<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>但其实我在监狱里也正好回顾了一下我之前对女主做的那些事<span><span>。</span></span>什么找小混混玷污女主的清白啦<span><span>，</span></span>什么恶意散播女主身世诋毁女主啦………</p>
 <p>手段简直是太低劣了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>当然<span><span>，</span></span>还包括前不久由我一手策划的车祸<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这些小手段不仅没有起到一点实质的作用<span><span>，</span></span>反而增强了男主对女主的保护欲和关爱<span><span>，</span></span>损人不利己<span><span>，</span></span>伤敌一百而自损了一千<span><span>，</span></span>简直愚蠢<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>反思过我此前的这些愚蠢行为后<span><span>，</span></span>我立志接下来当一个合格出色的恶毒女配<span><span>。</span></span>手段要玩得更高明<span><span>，</span></span>不然怎么配称恶毒女配呢<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p><strong>1</strong></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>茵茵<span><span>，</span></span>是妈妈来晚了<span><span>，</span></span>让你在这里受委屈了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我刚一走出监狱大门<span><span>，</span></span>一个贵妇模样的女人从轿车里冲了出来<span><span>，</span></span>一把抱住了我哭了起来<span><span>。</span></span>没错这是我的母亲<span><span>。</span></span>随后一个身着唐装<span><span>，</span></span>五十多岁的男人从轿车的另一边打开车门下来<span><span>，</span></span>眼角泛泪地说<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>没事就好<span><span>，</span></span>走吧<span><span>，</span></span>回家<span><span>」</span></span><span><span>。</span></span>这是我的父亲<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我看着眼前的父亲母亲<span><span>，</span></span>不知为何<span><span>，</span></span>心里有些触动<span><span>。</span></span>我是一个恶毒女配<span><span>，</span></span>但是我所有恶毒的资本以及作为女配的身家背景<span><span>、</span></span>学历样貌都是他们给我的<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我吸了吸鼻子<span><span>，</span></span>扶着母亲<span><span>，</span></span>说着<span><span>「</span></span>妈<span><span>，</span></span>别哭了<span><span>，</span></span>这不是应该高兴的吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>母亲抬起头<span><span>，</span></span>两眼的泪水止不住地往下流<span><span>，</span></span>嘴里还喃喃着<span><span>「</span></span>委屈我的茵茵了<span><span>，</span></span>委屈我的茵茵了……<span><span>」</span></span>我笑着摇摇头<span><span>，</span></span>用手擦了擦母亲脸上的泪水<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>回家吧<span><span>！</span></span>爸还在车边等着呢<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>母亲点点头<span><span>，</span></span>我搀着母亲向轿车走去<span><span>。</span></span>上了车<span><span>，</span></span>我与母亲一起坐在后座<span><span>，</span></span>一路上母亲一直拉着我的手不放<span><span>，</span></span>眼泪依旧止不住地流<span><span>，</span></span>嘴里也不停地说着<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>茵茵<span><span>，</span></span>我们不嫁了好吗<span><span>？</span></span>我们放弃吧<span><span>，</span></span>以咱们何家的家世<span><span>，</span></span>咱们不受这个委屈<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我们不嫁了<span><span>，</span></span>不嫁了<span><span>，</span></span>那婚约取消了就取消了<span><span>，</span></span>不嫁了<span><span>，</span></span>不嫁了……<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我笑着附和着<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>嗯嗯<span><span>，</span></span>不嫁了<span><span>，</span></span>我不嫁了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>心里却是暗想<span><span>，</span></span>呵<span><span>，</span></span>我可是恶毒女配<span><span>，</span></span>不嫁男主可以<span><span>，</span></span>可我怎么可能会让他们好过呢<span><span>？</span></span>不然这个剧情怎么发展下去<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>可男主是谁呢<span><span>？</span></span>他可是男主<span><span>，</span></span>我们面对这样一个带着主角光环的人<span><span>，</span></span>一定要知己知彼<span><span>。</span></span>那我们就来理一理这个所谓的男主<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他有个很俗套的名字<span><span>，</span></span>叫厉绍<span><span>，</span></span>一听这个姓就肯定是霸道总裁跑不了<span><span>。</span></span>厉家也是名门大家<span><span>，</span></span>历代从商从政的人不少<span><span>，</span></span>到了厉绍这一辈<span><span>，</span></span>积攒了不少家业<span><span>，</span></span>可就只有厉绍这么一个嫡出小辈<span><span>，</span></span>自然是享尽荣耀<span><span>。</span></span>而厉绍也是很对得起男主这个身份的<span><span>，</span></span>自小就出色<span><span>，</span></span>不管是学业还是打理家业<span><span>，</span></span>都是这几大家小辈中的佼佼者<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>跟男主一比<span><span>，</span></span>我这个女配……那必须是也没逊色多少<span><span>，</span></span>除了情商低了点以外<span><span>。</span></span>我们何家也算是书香门第<span><span>，</span></span>家里面历代都是读书人<span><span>，</span></span>并且每代大大小小的都有做官的族人<span><span>。</span></span>从我太爷爷那辈开始转为经商<span><span>，</span></span>怎么算也是有点家底的了<span><span>。</span></span>从爷爷这辈开始从政<span><span>，</span></span>虽然到我父亲这辈政局上根基还不稳<span><span>，</span></span>但是自古官商一家<span><span>，</span></span>我们家有钱<span><span>，</span></span>站稳不过是迟早的事<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>再说说我<span><span>，</span></span>国内名牌大学商学院毕业<span><span>，</span></span>又去外国读了经营管理专业博士<span><span>，</span></span>妥妥的一个高才生<span><span>。</span></span>智商方面没的说<span><span>，</span></span>就是处事上……算了这都是小事<span><span>，</span></span>总之就是从各个方面来看<span><span>，</span></span>我和男主都是门当户对<span><span>、</span></span>天造地设<span><span>，</span></span>怎么看怎么合适<span><span>。</span></span>所以厉家和何家两家大人们才同意我和厉绍订了婚<span><span>，</span></span>可是谁知道出来了一个女主<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>回到家里<span><span>，</span></span>我好奇地打量了一下何家<span><span>，</span></span>算是沿袭了前辈们书香门第的传统<span><span>，</span></span>并没有因为富贵了<span><span>，</span></span>而骄奢淫逸起来<span><span>。</span></span>父亲看我四处看<span><span>，</span></span>以为我是在找什么<span><span>，</span></span>便开口说道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不用找了<span><span>，</span></span>他是回来了<span><span>，</span></span>只不过我安排他去打点你出狱的事了<span><span>，</span></span>他做事你应该放心的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我点了点头<span><span>，</span></span>父亲口中的<span><span>「</span></span>他<span><span>」</span></span>是早年父亲和母亲从孤儿院带回来的养子——何树<span><span>，</span></span>虽然比我小三岁<span><span>，</span></span>但行事却很稳重果断<span><span>，</span></span>是父亲培养来帮助我将来打理家业的人<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我们从小一起长大<span><span>，</span></span>感情很好<span><span>。</span></span>只是不知道为什么<span><span>，</span></span>我和厉绍订婚以后何树就不太爱搭理我了<span><span>，</span></span>女主出现以后更是找了借口出国去了<span><span>。</span></span>这次估计是我进了监狱<span><span>，</span></span>父亲才急忙把他召回来为我打点出狱事宜<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>先生和夫人接小姐回来了<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>一个五十多岁的女人用围裙擦着手从厨房里出来<span><span>，</span></span>看到我十分激动<span><span>，</span></span>高兴地走过来拉住我的手<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>小姐<span><span>，</span></span>咱们别再犯傻了<span><span>，</span></span>那个厉家少爷再好咱们也不能搭上自己啊<span><span>！</span></span>小姐这么优秀一定可以找到更好的未婚夫的<span><span>，</span></span>咱们不稀罕他<span><span>，</span></span>可千万别再让先生和夫人担心了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>嗯<span><span>，</span></span>何姨<span><span>，</span></span>我已经想明白了<span><span>，</span></span>不会了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>这个女人是在何家多年的厨娘<span><span>，</span></span>算是看着我和何树长大的<span><span>。</span></span>当年母亲要管理家业无暇顾家<span><span>，</span></span>需要雇一个厨娘<span><span>，</span></span>正巧她也姓何<span><span>，</span></span>手脚又勤快<span><span>，</span></span>就留下了<span><span>，</span></span>谁知道一干就是二十多年<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>母亲看着何姨又看看我<span><span>，</span></span>走上前拍了拍何姨的手<span><span>，</span></span>说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>已经没事了<span><span>，</span></span>茵茵回来就好<span><span>，</span></span>何姐<span><span>，</span></span>饭好了吗<span><span>？</span></span>咱们赶紧开饭吧<span><span>，</span></span>那监狱哪像是人待的<span><span>，</span></span>茵茵一定吃也吃不好<span><span>，</span></span>睡也睡不好的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>何姨赞同地连连点头<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>就是就是<span><span>，</span></span>先生夫人小姐赶紧坐下<span><span>，</span></span>菜都烧好了<span><span>，</span></span>都是小姐爱吃的<span><span>，</span></span>我马上上菜<span><span>，</span></span>少爷说他晚点回来<span><span>，</span></span>让咱们不用等他<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>不知道为什么<span><span>，</span></span>看着眼前这温馨和谐的一幕<span><span>，</span></span>我甚至有点忘记我是恶毒女配的身份了<span><span>，</span></span>我可是要破坏男主女主的人<span><span>，</span></span>所以我一定是内心阴暗狠毒的人<span><span>，</span></span>但是如此温暖的家庭我是真的无法阴狠起来……融入这样的家庭<span><span>，</span></span>从此与男主女主再也不干涉不打扰不好吗<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>当然不好<span><span>！</span></span>我不能白白进监狱<span><span>，</span></span>被男主整<span><span>，</span></span>我要玩回来<span><span>，</span></span>不能辱没我恶毒女配的身份<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><strong>2</strong></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>咚咚咚<span><span>」</span></span>我迷迷糊糊听到有人敲门<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>谁啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>小姐<span><span>，</span></span>早餐已经做好了<span><span>，</span></span>先生和夫人已经在等了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>what<span><span>？</span></span>都在等了<span><span>？</span></span>难道在家不流行自然醒吗<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>我自然也不敢磨蹭<span><span>，</span></span>跳下床<span><span>，</span></span>套好衣服<span><span>，</span></span>飞速洗漱就冲下了楼<span><span>。</span></span>刚到楼梯口<span><span>，</span></span>果然看见何父何母已经在餐桌前坐好了<span><span>，</span></span>我不好意思地放慢脚步走了过去<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>何母看见我下来了<span><span>，</span></span>略带嗔怒地瞥了何父一眼说着<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你也是<span><span>，</span></span>茵茵才从那里出来<span><span>，</span></span>肯定要好好休息的<span><span>，</span></span>你倒好<span><span>，</span></span>还偏偏叫茵茵和以前一样的时间起床<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>说着还倒了杯牛奶递过来<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>茵茵昨晚睡得还好吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我愣了愣<span><span>，</span></span>点点头<span><span>，</span></span>接过牛奶<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>嗯<span><span>，</span></span>妈<span><span>，</span></span>没事<span><span>，</span></span>我睡得挺好的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>何父可能是看我今天气色不错<span><span>，</span></span>也笑了<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>虽说是应该多休息<span><span>，</span></span>但是咱们家的规矩不能乱<span><span>，</span></span>不能因为点小事把自家的礼数都忘了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>说着拿起筷子<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>动筷吧<span><span>，</span></span>小树还没回来<span><span>，</span></span>人齐了<span><span>，</span></span>就咱们仨<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我长吁了一口气<span><span>，</span></span>还好我先接了牛奶还不是先拿起筷子<span><span>。</span></span>怎么还有这种隐藏规则<span><span>？</span></span>何家不愧是书香门第啊<span><span>？</span></span>都 9012 年了还保留着应有的礼数<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>不对啊<span><span>，</span></span>那不应该啊<span><span>！</span></span>照理说我应该是家教极好的大家闺秀啊<span><span>，</span></span>就算是恶毒女配也应该是高端玩家<span><span>，</span></span>怎么会玩那些低端的手段<span><span>？</span></span>居然还把自己玩进了监狱<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>吃过饭<span><span>，</span></span>作为何家嫡长女<span><span>，</span></span>我自然要跟着何父去何家的企业学着管理家产<span><span>。</span></span>但是当我真的站在何家家族企业的公司大楼前时<span><span>，</span></span>我委实震惊了……光看外表就知道装修一定不便宜<span><span>，</span></span>还盖得这么高<span><span>，</span></span>一定花了不少钱吧<span><span>！</span></span>不是这何家这么有钱还差厉绍吗<span><span>？</span></span>厉绍能比何家有钱多少<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>可能是看我注视着高楼顶层发愣<span><span>，</span></span>何父又走到我身边拍了拍我的肩说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>茵茵<span><span>，</span></span>居高不胜寒<span><span>，</span></span>走吧<span><span>，</span></span>去办公室吧<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>什么<span><span>？</span></span>为什么突然来这么一句<span><span>？</span></span>我现在感觉我的智商也有点跟不上了<span><span>？</span></span>这是什么节奏<span><span>？</span></span>我一脸懵逼地跟着何父来到总裁办公室<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>直到我站在总裁办公室的落地窗前<span><span>，</span></span>我才明白了何父那句话的意思——何家将总裁办公室设在大厦的顶楼<span><span>，</span></span>一整层都是办公室<span><span>，</span></span>意在提醒每位何家的总裁<span><span>，</span></span>居高自危<span><span>，</span></span>身处高位的人总是孤独的<span><span>，</span></span>当然顶层也有掌控全局的意思<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>不过我真的是委实理解不了这个设计<span><span>，</span></span>在最高一层上班<span><span>，</span></span>这要是哪天倒霉发生个地震火灾什么的<span><span>，</span></span>岂不是第一个死的就是总裁了<span><span>？</span></span>何家总裁的危险系数也太高了吧<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>于是这一早上我就坐在总裁办公桌边梳理着何家的产业<span><span>，</span></span>何父则坐在旁边的沙发上喝茶看报纸<span><span>。</span></span>当然<span><span>，</span></span>顺便监督我<span><span>。</span></span>我这不看不要紧<span><span>，</span></span>一看真的是吓一跳<span><span>，</span></span>何家这动不动就几亿几亿的出账和进账<span><span>，</span></span>而且产业除了在主营的酒店行业<span><span>，</span></span>其他各个领域都或多或少有点涉猎 <span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我家这么有钱我还嫁什么厉绍啊<span><span>！</span></span>我自己不就是霸道总裁<span><span>？</span></span>我还不怕玩不死男主和女主<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p><strong>3</strong></p>
 <p>正当我为何家企业的资料而忙得头昏脑涨的时候<span><span>，</span></span>我的救星来了<span><span>，</span></span>即使前几天那个人还把我送进了监狱<span><span>。</span></span>没错就是我们的男主——厉绍<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>总裁<span><span>，</span></span>厉总来了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>门外传来秘书小姐温柔的提示音<span><span>，</span></span>我则抓住了关键词<span><span>「</span></span>厉总<span><span>」</span></span><span><span>？</span></span>哦嚯嚯<span><span>，</span></span>我正好要找他<span><span>，</span></span>他倒自己送上门来了<span><span>。</span></span>我看这次在我的地盘上<span><span>，</span></span>当着我爸的面<span><span>，</span></span>他怎么办<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>我放下手中的资料<span><span>，</span></span>看向何父<span><span>。</span></span>何父冷哼一声<span><span>，</span></span>小声说着<span><span>「</span></span>把我女儿送进监狱后还敢主动找过来<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我冲何父笑了笑表示没事<span><span>，</span></span>何父也只得点了点头<span><span>，</span></span>然后又继续看报纸<span><span>，</span></span>就好像只是一个员工要来汇报工作一样<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那就请厉总进来吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>话音刚落<span><span>，</span></span>总裁办公室的门就被推开了<span><span>，</span></span>一个身着黑色西装的男人走了进来<span><span>。</span></span>长得……嗯<span><span>，</span></span>怪不得我甘愿进监狱呢<span><span>！</span></span>确实长了张让人犯罪的脸<span><span>，</span></span>怎么办<span><span>，</span></span>我这个恶毒女配有点恶毒不起来了都要<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>厉绍走到我桌子前面敲了敲我的桌子<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何茵<span><span>，</span></span>回神了<span><span>，</span></span>这么看着我<span><span>，</span></span>你难道还想回去监狱待着<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我看着厉绍<span><span>，</span></span>妈呀<span><span>，</span></span>人什么时候都走到我面前了<span><span>，</span></span>他刚刚说什么<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>咳咳咳<span><span>，</span></span>厉贤侄倒是会说笑<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>何父放下手中的报纸<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>看来即使是我这个长辈坐在这里也不减贤侄的幽默感<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>何父语气平淡<span><span>，</span></span>可面色却冷峻<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>厉绍向何父看了一眼<span><span>，</span></span>点头不情愿地叫了声<span><span>「</span></span>何叔叔<span><span>」</span></span><span><span>，</span></span>然后后退了几步<span><span>，</span></span>面对何父说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何叔叔<span><span>，</span></span>这是我们小辈之间的事情<span><span>，</span></span>就不劳您费心了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我不由得咂咂嘴<span><span>，</span></span>不愧是男主<span><span>，</span></span>在人家的办公室请人家出去<span><span>，</span></span>这么霸道的吗<span><span>？</span></span>看来我这个恶毒女配不好当啊<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>何父有些生气地合上报纸<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>如果我没记错<span><span>，</span></span>这里好像是我何家的办公室吧<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我看见厉绍皱了皱眉<span><span>，</span></span>一副不满的表情<span><span>，</span></span>果然是被推崇惯了<span><span>。</span></span>他刚要开口<span><span>，</span></span>我就赶忙插话<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>爸<span><span>，</span></span>要不您先回去陪妈吧<span><span>！</span></span>是我约厉绍来的<span><span>，</span></span>我们待会找个咖啡厅谈谈就行<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><strong>4</strong></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>说吧<span><span>！</span></span>什么事<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>厉绍也不客气<span><span>，</span></span>长腿一跨在我对面的椅子上坐下了<span><span>，</span></span>双臂一环看着我<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我则站起身<span><span>，</span></span>收拾了一下文件说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>楼下有家咖啡厅<span><span>，</span></span>去那里聊吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>厉绍皱了皱眉<span><span>，</span></span>不耐烦地说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>有话快说<span><span>，</span></span>我没时间跟你喝咖啡<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我一听厉绍的语气<span><span>，</span></span>有点生气<span><span>，</span></span>你自己不请自来还让我有话快说<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span>不行<span><span>，</span></span>我恶毒女配不能掉面子<span><span>，</span></span>我一抬下巴<span><span>，</span></span>俯视着厉绍说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>厉绍<span><span>，</span></span>在这里聊<span><span>，</span></span>你不会想窃取我家商业机密吧<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说完我感觉厉绍的眼神都变了<span><span>，</span></span>但是我不能输<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>厉绍一脸看智障的表情看着我<span><span>，</span></span>然后不知道为什么突然笑了一下<span><span>，</span></span>说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>呵<span><span>，</span></span>就你家这几个市值不过十几个亿的小公司<span><span>，</span></span>我也就动动嘴的事<span><span>，</span></span>还需要商业机密<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>说罢厉绍从椅子上起来<span><span>，</span></span>走出办公室<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>楼下咖啡厅见<span><span>，</span></span>别让我等你<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>然后砰的一声关上了门<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我的天<span><span>，</span></span>这就是霸道总裁吗<span><span>？</span></span>也太霸道了吧<span><span>！</span></span>动动嘴就想让我家破产<span><span>，</span></span>他早上没睡醒吗<span><span>？</span></span>霸道总裁都有异想天开的技能吧<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>我摇了摇头<span><span>，</span></span>也走出办公室下去了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>在咖啡厅<span><span>，</span></span>我和厉绍坐了下来<span><span>，</span></span>店员好像认识我们一样<span><span>，</span></span>直接就上了一杯摩卡和一杯卡布奇诺<span><span>，</span></span>关键的是<span><span>！</span></span>厉绍喝卡布奇诺<span><span>！</span></span>这么甜腻腻的<span><span>，</span></span>居然是霸道总裁爱喝的<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>厉绍瞥了我一眼<span><span>，</span></span>说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>怎么<span><span>？</span></span>你忘了<span><span>？</span></span>姣姣爱喝这个的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>姣姣<span><span>？</span></span>哦哦哦<span><span>，</span></span>想起来<span><span>，</span></span>我们的女主祝姣<span><span>，</span></span>对对对<span><span>，</span></span>征服了霸道总裁的女人<span><span>。</span></span>啧啧啧<span><span>，</span></span>可以让霸道总裁记住她的喜好<span><span>，</span></span>看来不简单<span><span>，</span></span>怪不得我一开始没斗过她<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>没事<span><span>，</span></span>开始吧<span><span>！</span></span>谈什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我突然正经起来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>行<span><span>，</span></span>我直说了<span><span>，</span></span>婚约不能解除<span><span>，</span></span>咱俩正常举行婚礼<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>说着厉绍还喝了一口卡布奇诺<span><span>，</span></span>明明都皱眉嫌弃了<span><span>，</span></span>却还是又喝了一口<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>excuse me<span><span>？</span></span>是我耳朵有问题还是厉绍脑子有问题<span><span>？</span></span>不解除婚约他怎么跟祝姣结婚<span><span>？</span></span>难道他要放弃女主了<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你决定放弃祝姣了<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我小心地问着<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你在做梦吧<span><span>？</span></span>我放弃姣姣选择你吗<span><span>？</span></span>你是不是监狱没待够<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你说不解除婚约的<span><span>，</span></span>那我不往你放弃祝姣上面想我才是脑子有问题呢<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>厉绍一口喝完卡布奇诺<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>行行行<span><span>，</span></span>是我没说清楚<span><span>，</span></span>今天呢就是想跟你说一下<span><span>，</span></span>我是这样计划的<span><span>，</span></span>我<span><span>，</span></span>还正常跟你举行婚礼<span><span>，</span></span>但是咱俩不领证<span><span>，</span></span>结婚以后也不同居<span><span>，</span></span>我跟姣姣领证同居<span><span>，</span></span>你看这样怎么样<span><span>？</span></span>既满足你嫁给我了<span><span>，</span></span>又不拆散我和姣姣<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>hetui<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span>什么霸道总裁<span><span>，</span></span>明明就是一个渣男<span><span>！</span></span>脚踏两条船<span><span>，</span></span>什么烂计划<span><span>，</span></span>傻子才同意呢<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>厉大少爷<span><span>，</span></span>你才在做梦呢吧<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我冷哼一声<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>牺牲我的大好时光和未来幸福跟你结婚<span><span>，</span></span>最后我还不受法律保护<span><span>，</span></span>捞不到一分钱<span><span>，</span></span>白便宜了祝姣<span><span>，</span></span>哪有这么做买卖的<span><span>，</span></span>我又不傻<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>可以啊<span><span>，</span></span>监狱没白蹲<span><span>，</span></span>倒是比以前冷静了点<span><span>，</span></span>有点商学院高才生的感觉了哈<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>厉绍说着点点头<span><span>，</span></span>然后突然拍桌而起<span><span>，</span></span>向我吼着<span><span>「</span></span>你要是不同意别找我妈来压我啊<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我被吓了一跳<span><span>，</span></span>我找厉夫人威胁厉绍<span><span>？</span></span>怎么可能<span><span>！</span></span>我站起来正了正自己的衣服看着厉绍说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你不是霸道总裁吗<span><span>？</span></span>有本事你查查我<span><span>，</span></span>看我出狱以来见没见过你妈<span><span>、</span></span>打没打过电话<span><span>。</span></span>连点证据都没有你平白无故就说是我<span><span>，</span></span>厉绍<span><span>，</span></span>脑子呢<span><span>？</span></span>你三岁啊<span><span>？</span></span>厉家在你这样的人的带领下估计发展还不如我家这几家小公司吧<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>扬眉吐气<span><span>，</span></span>爽<span><span>！</span></span>让你送我进监狱<span><span>！</span></span>怼霸道总裁就是爽<span><span>。</span></span>原来霸道总裁只会霸道<span><span>，</span></span>智商都跟不上啊<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>厉绍也许是意识到了<span><span>，</span></span>有些面子挂不住地坐下了<span><span>，</span></span>语气都有点缓和了<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>真不是你<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我大大方方地一坐<span><span>，</span></span>喝了一口咖啡<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我巴不得跟你解除婚约呢<span><span>！</span></span>未婚妻都能送进监狱<span><span>，</span></span>谁知道结婚后会不会家暴<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你……<span><span>」</span></span>厉绍刚想生气<span><span>，</span></span>又笑了笑<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>很好<span><span>，</span></span>进过监狱的人就是不一样<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>一言不合就提监狱<span><span>，</span></span>有毒吧<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你也可以进去感受感受<span><span>，</span></span>没准能聪明点<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>这回厉绍没生气<span><span>，</span></span>反而向后一靠<span><span>，</span></span>双腿一叠<span><span>，</span></span>问我<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>这种事就不向何小姐看齐了<span><span>，</span></span>既然何小姐看得这么透彻<span><span>，</span></span>那你说怎么办<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>怎么办<span><span>？</span></span>还能怎么办<span><span>，</span></span>解除婚约啊<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>可我还没开口<span><span>，</span></span>厉绍就先给我泼了盆冷水<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>婚约是解除不了了<span><span>，</span></span>消息都放出去好久了<span><span>，</span></span>你我两家因为联姻这事做了不少项目<span><span>，</span></span>股价涨了不少<span><span>，</span></span>突然解除<span><span>，</span></span>这损失何小姐不会算不出来<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我细细合计了一下<span><span>，</span></span>厉绍说得有道理<span><span>，</span></span>万一我家股票真的跌了怎么办<span><span>？</span></span>一时半会我还没有什么措施可以挽回股价<span><span>，</span></span>不合算不合算<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>这样吧<span><span>，</span></span>你跟我结婚领证<span><span>，</span></span>不同居<span><span>，</span></span>我可以接受你和祝姣在外面一起生活<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>到时候把消息捅出去<span><span>，</span></span>凭我这演技<span><span>，</span></span>让你俩身败名裂不成问题<span><span>。</span></span>哼哼<span><span>，</span></span>敢让我蹲监狱<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不行<span><span>，</span></span>姣姣必须有名分<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那你给我钱吧<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我立马说<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>作为嫁给你却没有资格分你家家产的青春损失费<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>这下换厉绍蒙圈了<span><span>？</span></span>一脸懵逼地看着我<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你缺钱<span><span>？</span></span>还是何家出事了<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我不能白浪费自己的青春时光<span><span>，</span></span>没有利益的事我不干<span><span>。</span></span>再说了<span><span>，</span></span>我还没到嫁不出去的地步吧<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我也跷起二郎腿<span><span>，</span></span>手指敲着桌子<span><span>，</span></span>摆出一副谈判的样子<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>行<span><span>，</span></span>也只能这样了<span><span>，</span></span>你说<span><span>，</span></span>多少<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我笑了笑<span><span>，</span></span>开口<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>少了就体现不出来咱们厉总裁霸道总裁的身份了<span><span>，</span></span>不如就这个数吧<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我比了个数字给厉绍看<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>两百万<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>呸<span><span>，</span></span>才两百万你做梦呢<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>看来厉总没什么诚意啊<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我佯作失望地摇摇头<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>两亿<span><span>？</span></span>何茵你觉得你值这个价吗<span><span>？</span></span>我两亿买个花瓶在家摆着还好看呢<span><span>，</span></span>买个你能干吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>没眼光<span><span>！</span></span>是你们厉家百分之二十的股份<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>厉绍震惊地看着我<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>谁给你的胆子想动我们家产业<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我也不甘示弱地回应<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>谁给你的胆子敢让我白嫁给你<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>少一点<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你买菜呢<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>百分之二<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>百分之十五<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>百分之十<span><span>，</span></span>不能再多了<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>成交<span><span>，</span></span>咱俩写个协议<span><span>，</span></span>你就当聘礼送到我家<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你真的比以前精明了<span><span>，</span></span>以前还想用何家当嫁妆<span><span>，</span></span>要死要活地要嫁我来着<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>以前眼瞎<span><span>，</span></span>现在治好了<span><span>。</span></span>行<span><span>，</span></span>那就这么说定了<span><span>，</span></span>我回去敲份协议出来<span><span>，</span></span>咱俩找个时间签一下<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我站起来准备走<span><span>，</span></span>又转身提醒厉绍<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>越少人知道越好<span><span>，</span></span>你妈我妈他们更不能说<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>放心<span><span>，</span></span>我脑子有问题啊<span><span>，</span></span>告诉他们<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>合作愉快<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>合作愉快……<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><strong>5</strong></p>
 <p>今天<span><span>，</span></span>真的是值得纪念的一天<span><span>，</span></span>至于为什么<span><span>，</span></span>你听我跟你讲……</p>
 <p>既然和厉绍协议结婚<span><span>，</span></span>那么我俩的合作关系算是暂时达成了<span><span>，</span></span>关系也缓和不少<span><span>。</span></span>这不<span><span>，</span></span>为了向外界表示我们的关系有所改善<span><span>，</span></span>厉绍这个霸道总裁很大方地带着我这个恶毒女配进行了很多商业合作<span><span>，</span></span>来进行他认为的<span><span>「</span></span>秀恩爱<span><span>」</span></span>……</p>
 <p>呸<span><span>，</span></span>渣男<span><span>，</span></span>合作的项目他也没少赚<span><span>，</span></span>表现得那么大方干吗<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>所以今天我以何家当家人以及厉绍的未婚妻的身份应邀参加 X 市的企业家聚会<span><span>，</span></span>无非就是互相认识<span><span>，</span></span>多个朋友多个关系多条路的见面会<span><span>。</span></span>反正也没什么坏处<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>当我挽着厉绍<span><span>，</span></span>一脸笑着走进大厅的时候<span><span>，</span></span>我感觉大家都在看我<span><span>。</span></span>作为一个恶毒女配<span><span>，</span></span>我当然要委婉地表现出很幸福<span><span>。</span></span>所以我端着我那标准的大家闺秀笑<span><span>，</span></span>小声低头对厉绍说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>哎呀<span><span>，</span></span>阿绍<span><span>，</span></span>我脚疼<span><span>，</span></span>可不可以去你包间休息一下啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>当然<span><span>，</span></span>这个声音虽然小<span><span>，</span></span>但必须被身边的人听见<span><span>，</span></span>不然怎么体现出我的身份<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何茵<span><span>，</span></span>你又搞什么<span><span>？</span></span>今天姣姣也在<span><span>，</span></span>我警告你<span><span>，</span></span>别太过分了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>厉绍冷着他的脸<span><span>，</span></span>小声警告我<span><span>，</span></span>估计是没好意思拂我脸面<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>什么<span><span>？</span></span>女主也在<span><span>？</span></span>她是企业家吗<span><span>！</span></span>她什么理由来啊<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>我笑着咬牙说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那我原话送给你<span><span>，</span></span>别跟祝姣做什么让我丢脸的事<span><span>，</span></span>不然咱俩一拍两散<span><span>，</span></span>两败俱伤<span><span>，</span></span>谁怕谁<span><span>？</span></span>快扶我去你的包间<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不是说厉绍前几天刚把何茵送进监狱吗<span><span>？</span></span>还是亲手送进去的<span><span>，</span></span>怎么现在关系这么好<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>估计是打情骂俏吧<span><span>。</span></span>你看人家俩现在这个感情<span><span>，</span></span>多好啊<span><span>！</span></span>而且马上就要举办婚礼了<span><span>，</span></span>日子都定好了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>有钱人的恋爱咱们懂什么啊<span><span>？</span></span>小说里不都这么写<span><span>，</span></span>进进监狱<span><span>，</span></span>失失忆<span><span>，</span></span>出出车祸才能大结局啊<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>bingo<span><span>！</span></span>看来我和厉绍这种小对话在旁人眼里就是悄悄话啊<span><span>！</span></span>OK<span><span>，</span></span>目的也算达到一点了<span><span>。</span></span>我端着<span><span>「</span></span>幸福<span><span>」</span></span>的架子挽着厉绍的手臂从他们身边经过<span><span>，</span></span>一句话却隐隐约约地传入我的耳中……</p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>看这何茵恢复得不错啊<span><span>！</span></span>两个月前的车祸倒是一点后遗症都没留下<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>什么<span><span>？</span></span>我还出过车祸吗<span><span>？</span></span>我怎么不记得了<span><span>？</span></span>两个月前的什么时候<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>走到了为几大家安排的包间走廊上<span><span>，</span></span>已经没什么人了<span><span>，</span></span>我好奇<span><span>，</span></span>刚想问厉绍车祸的事<span><span>，</span></span>身后突然传来一个声音<span><span>，</span></span>一个女人的声音……</p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>阿绍<span><span>，</span></span>等你挺久了<span><span>，</span></span>怎么才来<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>厉绍一听赶忙松开我的手臂<span><span>，</span></span>转身<span><span>，</span></span>声音都温柔了<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>姣姣<span><span>，</span></span>怎么在这里等我啊<span><span>？</span></span>我刚刚在宴厅找你半天还以为你没来呢<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我的内心警铃大作<span><span>，</span></span>女主<span><span>！</span></span>身后这个是女主<span><span>！</span></span>虽然我早就预料到会和女主在宴会上碰见<span><span>，</span></span>但是这也太早了吧<span><span>！</span></span>周围还没有什么目击者<span><span>，</span></span>只有个霸道总裁的厉绍<span><span>，</span></span>我怎么发挥我恶毒女配的作用啊<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你邀请我<span><span>，</span></span>我肯定要来啊<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>那个声音突然一顿<span><span>，</span></span>我听着她好像走了几步<span><span>，</span></span>离我应该是近了一点<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>怎么<span><span>？</span></span>何茵你还对我有恨意吗<span><span>？</span></span>恨阿绍为我把你送进监狱<span><span>？</span></span>难道你对我做的那些事你就没有一点愧疚吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>说着说着还有点哽咽<span><span>，</span></span>厉绍赶紧走过去<span><span>，</span></span>揽住祝姣的肩<span><span>，</span></span>小声安慰<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我深吸了一口气<span><span>，</span></span>大大方方地转过身<span><span>，</span></span>刚想开口<span><span>，</span></span>面前这一幕恩爱的场景却有些刺眼<span><span>。</span></span>我有些激动<span><span>，</span></span>想把两个人拉开<span><span>，</span></span>又有些不甘心<span><span>，</span></span>为什么我是一个恶毒女配啊<span><span>！</span></span>我也想要甜甜的爱情<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>但我还是平复了一下心情<span><span>，</span></span>很温柔地回答<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>恨啊<span><span>，</span></span>怎么不恨<span><span>，</span></span>你抢走了我的未婚夫<span><span>，</span></span>抢走了本来属于我的天作之合<span><span>，</span></span>比起这个<span><span>，</span></span>我做的那些算什么呢<span><span>？</span></span>你得到了我的世界<span><span>，</span></span>还不允许我象征性地反抗一下吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何茵<span><span>！</span></span>你别太过分<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>厉绍突然语气强烈地吼我<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我瞥了厉绍一眼<span><span>，</span></span>没理他<span><span>。</span></span>又继续说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>看<span><span>，</span></span>本来属于我的盾去保护别的女孩了<span><span>，</span></span>我还不能去挽留一下<span><span>。</span></span>你有什么可怜的啊<span><span>，</span></span>咱俩比起来明明我更可怜吧……<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你明明什么都有<span><span>，</span></span>还跟我抢阿绍干嘛<span><span>！</span></span>而且阿绍选择我<span><span>，</span></span>是阿绍自己的决定<span><span>，</span></span>你怪我什么呢<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>祝姣一下子就流泪了<span><span>，</span></span>本来就娇小可人的样子<span><span>，</span></span>哭起来更是梨花带雨的<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>厉绍一看祝姣流泪了<span><span>，</span></span>立马就急眼了<span><span>，</span></span>狠狠地瞪着我<span><span>，</span></span>威胁道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>够了<span><span>！</span></span>何茵<span><span>，</span></span>没你事了<span><span>，</span></span>别忘记咱俩的协议<span><span>，</span></span>现在赶紧滚回何家的包间<span><span>，</span></span>不然我今天可保证不了你还能体体面面地走出这个宴会厅<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>看啊<span><span>，</span></span>她刚刚流了点眼泪你就心疼了<span><span>，</span></span>我被抛弃了这么久也没有你的怜悯<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>呵<span><span>，</span></span>什么协议也改变不了你要向众人宣告你娶我的事实<span><span>，</span></span>而她<span><span>，</span></span>你的姣姣<span><span>，</span></span>连站在你身边接受众人祝福的资格都没有<span><span>。</span></span>未来你要出席的所有宴会<span><span>、</span></span>聚会<span><span>，</span></span>以及洽谈的合作所需要的厉夫人只能是我<span><span>，</span></span>也只能是我挽着你的手臂进场<span><span>，</span></span>祝姣她配吗<span><span>？</span></span>一辈子<span><span>，</span></span>她一辈子都不配<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我顿了顿<span><span>，</span></span>给自己壮了壮胆子<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>厉绍<span><span>，</span></span>说什么你爱祝姣<span><span>，</span></span>你现在能做的就是像养情妇一样<span><span>，</span></span>让祝姣活在你的身后<span><span>。</span></span>呵<span><span>，</span></span>这样的爱情<span><span>，</span></span>懦弱无能<span><span>，</span></span>我何茵一点都不稀罕<span><span>，</span></span>一点都不想要<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>厉绍听后终于再也绷不住了<span><span>，</span></span>他松开祝姣向我走来<span><span>，</span></span>抬手就要打我<span><span>。</span></span>我不甘示弱地那么站着<span><span>，</span></span>瞪着眼看着厉绍<span><span>，</span></span>内心却慌乱得一批<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>完了完了<span><span>，</span></span>太冲动了<span><span>，</span></span>我可是高端玩家的<span><span>！</span></span>怎么又打烂牌<span><span>，</span></span>现在撕破脸一点好处都没有的<span><span>！</span></span>好不容易缓和的关系又崩塌了<span><span>。</span></span>凉了凉了<span><span>，</span></span>何茵啊<span><span>！</span></span>脑子怎么又好像不见了呢<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>刚刚的话就好像是提前准备好的剧本<span><span>，</span></span>映在我的脑海了<span><span>，</span></span>我就像是读下来的一样<span><span>，</span></span>一气呵成<span><span>，</span></span>声情并茂<span><span>，</span></span>抑扬顿挫<span><span>。</span></span>不知道为什么<span><span>，</span></span>这居然不受我理智的控制<span><span>，</span></span>就好像我必须要做出来<span><span>，</span></span>有什么神秘的力量控制我一样<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我站着等待厉绍的巴掌<span><span>，</span></span>我感觉它近了<span><span>，</span></span>耳旁好像已经能听到手掌带起来的风了<span><span>，</span></span>我轻轻地闭上眼<span><span>，</span></span>心想<span><span>：</span></span>这下回家要让何姨准备蛋清消肿了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这个巴掌扇的时间有点长啊<span><span>？</span></span>我闭着眼等了好几秒<span><span>，</span></span>耳旁的风都停了<span><span>，</span></span>可巴掌还没落<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>excuse me<span><span>？</span></span>我期待已久的巴掌呢<span><span>？</span></span>厉绍良心突然发现吗<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>就是这时<span><span>，</span></span>一个声音在我身边响起<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>别碰她<span><span>，</span></span>你不配<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>哦嚯嚯<span><span>，</span></span>英雄救美的事情终于落到我身上了<span><span>，</span></span>我可以拥有甜甜的爱情了吗<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>我赶紧睁开眼<span><span>，</span></span>只看见厉绍的手在另一只手的紧握下<span><span>，</span></span>停在了我脸旁<span><span>，</span></span>晚一秒<span><span>，</span></span>结果就不一样了<span><span>。</span></span>我抬头看向那只手的主人<span><span>，</span></span>想表达谢意却发现……那人我认识<span><span>，</span></span>是……是我最最亲爱的弟弟<span><span>，</span></span>何树<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>小树<span><span>？</span></span>你怎么也来了<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我赶紧分开两个人的手<span><span>，</span></span>惊喜地拉过何树<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>厉绍咬牙切齿地看着何树<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>怎么<span><span>，</span></span>现在想起来她是你姐了<span><span>，</span></span>早干嘛去了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>厉绍看见何树到了<span><span>，</span></span>也不多停留了<span><span>，</span></span>转身拉着祝姣进了厉家的包间<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>姐<span><span>，</span></span>没事吧<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>何树反抓住我<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>还好我到了<span><span>，</span></span>还好<span><span>，</span></span>不然你又要被姓厉的欺负了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>然后不知原因地抱住了我<span><span>，</span></span>安慰着<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>其实我也没什么委屈的<span><span>，</span></span>我推推何树说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我没什么事<span><span>，</span></span>刚刚的话确实说得过分了<span><span>，</span></span>厉绍要打我也是意料之中的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>何树轻轻地拍着我的背<span><span>，</span></span>听似责怪<span><span>，</span></span>实则温柔地问我<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那为什么不躲呢<span><span>？</span></span>就这么喜欢他吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我忘了<span><span>，</span></span>说实话<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>何树笑了<span><span>，</span></span>松开我<span><span>，</span></span>他看着我的眼睛<span><span>，</span></span>突然认真地问<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>是因为喜欢才忘的吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>额……这个话题没完了<span><span>。</span></span>我眨了眨眼睛<span><span>，</span></span>赶紧开始转移话题<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你从我订婚起就离开家<span><span>，</span></span>许久未见了<span><span>，</span></span>来让姐好好看看<span><span>。</span></span>咱们姐弟好好叙叙旧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我拉着何树走向何家的包间<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>何树苦笑着摇摇头<span><span>，</span></span>小声回应着<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>好<span><span>，</span></span>那就姐弟叙旧吧<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>宴会终于进行到关键环节<span><span>，</span></span>我和厉绍作为几大家中厉<span><span>、</span></span>何两家的当家人自然不能缺席了<span><span>。</span></span>但是刚刚又闹得那么僵<span><span>，</span></span>这次又怎么好意思一起再亲密地手挽手出现呢<span><span>？</span></span>真是伤脑筋<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我自然拉不下脸去找厉绍求和<span><span>，</span></span>厉绍也肯定不会轻易原谅我<span><span>。</span></span>索性我也不装了<span><span>，</span></span>挽着何树算了<span><span>，</span></span>我弟弟长得又不差<span><span>，</span></span>标标准准高富帅<span><span>，</span></span>还没有霸道总裁的蛮不讲理<span><span>，</span></span>我也不亏<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我挽着何树的手<span><span>，</span></span>我们互相吐槽这会场的装潢<span><span>、</span></span>菜品<span><span>，</span></span>以及互相介绍到场的人<span><span>，</span></span>有说有笑地进了大厅<span><span>。</span></span>举办宴会的人可能是听了我和厉绍订婚在即的消息了<span><span>，</span></span>居然把厉家和何家的席位安排在了一起<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>我看着厉绍身旁坐着祝姣在那个位置<span><span>，</span></span>咂咂嘴<span><span>，</span></span>突然有点不好意思过去<span><span>。</span></span>可能是感觉到了我的尴尬<span><span>，</span></span>何树拍了拍我的手说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>姐<span><span>，</span></span>没事<span><span>，</span></span>有我呢<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>然后何树拉着我走向何家的席位<span><span>，</span></span>毫不犹豫地坐到了厉绍的旁边<span><span>，</span></span>把我安排在了他的身边<span><span>。</span></span>也好<span><span>，</span></span>这样也好<span><span>，</span></span>现在也只能这样了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>有些人可能看出来我们和厉绍的尴尬局面<span><span>，</span></span>居然还调侃地问着何树<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>哎哟<span><span>，</span></span>何少爷这是刚回来没听到消息吧<span><span>？</span></span>何小姐马上就要跟厉总订婚了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>潜台词再清楚不过了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我看了何树一眼<span><span>，</span></span>何树倒是没有一丝慌乱<span><span>，</span></span>不紧不慢地说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>这个我知道<span><span>，</span></span>也不是什么大事<span><span>。</span></span>只不过我姐作为一个女士<span><span>，</span></span>穿着这么漂亮的晚礼裙<span><span>，</span></span>还踩着那么高的高跟鞋<span><span>，</span></span>本来进进出出的就不方便<span><span>，</span></span>再挨着厉总坐里面的话……等到上台发言的时候<span><span>，</span></span>恐怕就更耽误时间了<span><span>。</span></span>还是我和厉总多交流吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>何树狠狠地咬下了<span><span>「</span></span>厉总<span><span>」</span></span><span><span>，</span></span>还瞥了厉绍一眼<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我在一旁笑着点头<span><span>，</span></span>那人看没趣就讪笑着走开了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我向我另一边的座位看着<span><span>，</span></span>上面写着<span><span>「</span></span>叶<span><span>」</span></span><span><span>，</span></span>这一家我知道<span><span>，</span></span>近几年才闯出名头的<span><span>，</span></span>也没什么坚实的背景<span><span>，</span></span>就是跟我爸平辈的那一代贩点东西<span><span>，</span></span>算是个暴发户<span><span>。</span></span>不过在我们这一辈里那个叶万山倒是有点名头<span><span>，</span></span>是军部的<span><span>，</span></span>也不知道他爹一个暴发户怎么把自己儿子弄进军部这个好地方的<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我闭上眼<span><span>，</span></span>养神<span><span>，</span></span>同时也准备着随后上台的发言<span><span>。</span></span>这时耳边传来窸窸窣窣的衣服摩擦声<span><span>，</span></span>我身边的位置好像坐下了一个人<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>出于礼貌我睁开眼<span><span>，</span></span>端起我那名门闺秀的笑容<span><span>，</span></span>看向那个人<span><span>。</span></span>应该就是那个叶万山吧<span><span>？</span></span>呸<span><span>，</span></span>肯定是了<span><span>，</span></span>这种场合还穿着军装的还能有几个<span><span>！</span></span>这男人长得也不错啊<span><span>！</span></span>我没什么文学功底<span><span>，</span></span>说不出来长得多好看<span><span>，</span></span>反正就是一个很好看的兵哥哥就对了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>好久不见啊<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我也不知道自己为什么会说出来这样的话<span><span>，</span></span>我跟他好像印象中一点也不熟吧<span><span>？</span></span>应该都没有见过几次吧<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>好久不见<span><span>，</span></span>何小姐<span><span>」</span></span>叶万山也没感到什么奇怪<span><span>，</span></span>居然也很自然而然地回应我<span><span>，</span></span>声音有些低沉却富有磁性<span><span>，</span></span>我的天<span><span>，</span></span>这绝对是一个军宠文的男主标配啊<span><span>！</span></span>怎么活成这个霸道总裁的路人甲<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>我正想继续开展什么话题<span><span>，</span></span>却只见席间风风火火地坐进来一个小姑娘<span><span>，</span></span>大概二十一二的样子<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>哥你怎么不等我啊<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>然后她看了我一眼<span><span>，</span></span>震惊地说着<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>原来是何茵姐在啊<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>然后又瞥了叶万山一眼<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>怪不得呢<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>嗯<span><span>？</span></span>局面有点迷之……我有点不知道怎么进行下去了<span><span>。</span></span>我跟这叶家的兄妹熟吗<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>轻舟<span><span>，</span></span>别胡说<span><span>，</span></span>我不知道何小姐坐这里<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶万山淡淡地说<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那你起开<span><span>，</span></span>我跟何茵姐聊<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>小姑娘也不客气<span><span>，</span></span>直接就拉叶万山<span><span>，</span></span>让叶万山和她交换位置<span><span>。</span></span>叶万山无奈地摇摇头<span><span>，</span></span>站了起来<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我去下卫生间<span><span>，</span></span>你别乱跑<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>好好好<span><span>，</span></span>你去吧<span><span>，</span></span>去吧<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>小姑娘摆摆手<span><span>，</span></span>很自然地坐在了叶万山的位置上<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你就是叶轻舟吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>嗯嗯<span><span>，</span></span>是的<span><span>，</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>还记得我<span><span>，</span></span>真好<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟显得很激动<span><span>，</span></span>就好像一个小迷妹一样看着我<span><span>，</span></span>让我有点不好意思<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>想来令尊的文化修养也是极高的<span><span>，</span></span>万山拥水伴轻舟<span><span>，</span></span>真的是一幅很美的山水画呢<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我躲不过叶轻舟小迷妹般的眼神<span><span>，</span></span>急于岔开话题<span><span>，</span></span>便欣赏起叶家兄妹的名字<span><span>。</span></span>说实话<span><span>，</span></span>比起我和何树的名字<span><span>，</span></span>我感觉叶万山和叶轻舟才更像是书香人家出身的吧<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哪有啊<span><span>，</span></span>我爸他啊才是大老粗一个<span><span>，</span></span>就像一个土财主一样<span><span>，</span></span>有什么文化啊<span><span>！</span></span>我和哥的名字是当时一个跟爸要好的叔叔起的<span><span>，</span></span>那个叔叔还给我家送了一幅画呢<span><span>，</span></span>好像就是何茵姐你说的那样的画<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟倒是活泼<span><span>，</span></span>丝毫不介意自己父亲暴发户的身份<span><span>，</span></span>倒不像其他几家<span><span>，</span></span>巴不得祖上几代都为官为商<span><span>，</span></span>恨不得跟所有出点名的先人攀点亲呢<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>我说话直你别生气<span><span>，</span></span>我真的觉得你和那个什么祝姣都不是一个级别的<span><span>，</span></span>你怎么会被她给抢了未婚夫啊<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟小声地问我<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我爸从小就跟我说<span><span>，</span></span>说何家的女儿怎么样怎么样<span><span>，</span></span>我从小就崇拜你<span><span>，</span></span>我感觉你好厉害<span><span>，</span></span>长得好<span><span>，</span></span>学习好<span><span>，</span></span>家世还好<span><span>，</span></span>怎么就这么让那个祝姣比下去了<span><span>，</span></span>我超级为你不服<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说着说着叶轻舟语气还开始激动了起来<span><span>，</span></span>看起来不像是装的<span><span>，</span></span>倒真的像是为我打抱不平一样<span><span>。</span></span>我也没生气<span><span>，</span></span>笑着拍拍她的手<span><span>，</span></span>说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>没什么服不服<span><span>，</span></span>感情这种事<span><span>，</span></span>有时候真的跟家世<span><span>、</span></span>相貌没什么关系<span><span>，</span></span>就是一个感觉<span><span>，</span></span>感觉对了<span><span>，</span></span>怎么样都行<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶轻舟看我这么淡然<span><span>，</span></span>也平静了一下<span><span>，</span></span>有点不满地说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我要遇见这种事<span><span>，</span></span>我肯定不能认啊<span><span>！</span></span>我可做不到何茵姐你这样大度<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>所以呢<span><span>？</span></span>轻舟有未婚夫吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>叶轻舟终于有了点小女孩的羞涩<span><span>，</span></span>低下头<span><span>，</span></span>摇了摇<span><span>，</span></span>小声说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>没有呢<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我笑着顺了顺叶轻舟的头发<span><span>，</span></span>开玩笑道<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我猜也是<span><span>，</span></span>要不然未婚夫不铁定要怕死啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>啊<span><span>？</span></span>我这么凶吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>当然不是<span><span>，</span></span>轻舟这样很活泼会有很多人喜欢的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>也不知道为什么<span><span>，</span></span>我就这么叫着叶轻舟<span><span>，</span></span>感觉很熟悉<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>叶轻舟终于安安静静地坐在椅子上<span><span>，</span></span>时不时看看我<span><span>，</span></span>时不时看看台子上的人<span><span>，</span></span>好像想说什么<span><span>，</span></span>又不好意思说的样子<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>终于到我上台代表何家致辞了<span><span>，</span></span>我提着裙子一步步稳稳地登上台子<span><span>，</span></span>优雅地站在话筒前<span><span>。</span></span>我将何茵作为何家大小姐应该优秀的样子摆给台下人<span><span>。</span></span>当然<span><span>，</span></span>我那看似即兴发挥<span><span>，</span></span>实则精心准备许久的发言也算在内<span><span>。</span></span>最起码我的一举一动<span><span>，</span></span>举手投足都要展现出我该有的样子<span><span>，</span></span>不能让他们把我和进监狱<span><span>、</span></span>被抢未婚夫的落魄何茵联系起来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>恶毒女配<span><span>，</span></span>就是应该走到哪都要有排面<span><span>，</span></span>不管怎样都要端好我高端玩家的样子<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>当我结束发言<span><span>，</span></span>施施然回到座位<span><span>，</span></span>叶轻舟止不住地夸我<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何茵姐你好有气质<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>啊啊啊<span><span>，</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>我好想变成你<span><span>，</span></span>你太好看了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何茵姐你真的好棒<span><span>，</span></span>厉绍那个傻子没选你真的是眼瞎啊<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何茵姐你嫁给我哥吧<span><span>，</span></span>我哥很优秀的<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>……</p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>闭嘴<span><span>！</span></span>你好吵<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我刚想开口阻止叶轻舟接下来的话<span><span>，</span></span>却被何树抢先了<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>谁想嫁给你哥啊<span><span>？</span></span>我姐这么优秀你哥配吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你……你<span><span>，</span></span>我哥也很优秀<span><span>，</span></span>也很帅啊<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟瞪着何树<span><span>，</span></span>何树也瞪着她<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我一看场面不对<span><span>，</span></span>赶紧推了推何树<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>小树<span><span>，</span></span>闹着玩呢 =<span><span>，</span></span>别这么认真<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>姐<span><span>，</span></span>他们都配不上你<span><span>。</span></span>真的<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>何树又突然看着我<span><span>，</span></span>认真地说<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你要有这个自觉<span><span>，</span></span>厉绍没选择你是对的<span><span>，</span></span>因为他不配<span><span>，</span></span>没人配得上你<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>完了<span><span>，</span></span>好好的孩子怎么长成个姐控啊<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那我总不能一辈子不嫁人吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我半开玩笑说<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我……<span><span>」</span></span>何树欲言又止<span><span>，</span></span>安静地靠在椅背上不说话了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我也没再理何树了<span><span>，</span></span>转头对叶轻舟说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>既然从小就崇拜我<span><span>，</span></span>那要不要跟着我学习啊<span><span>？</span></span>我亲自教你怎么变成叶茵啊<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>真的吗<span><span>？</span></span>何茵姐不嫌我烦愿意带着我玩吗<span><span>？</span></span>好啊好啊<span><span>，</span></span>我太愿意了<span><span>！</span></span>何茵姐你真好<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟疯狂点头<span><span>，</span></span>然后隔着椅子抱住我<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我笑着回抱着她<span><span>，</span></span>高端的恶毒女配一定要有几个小跟班啊<span><span>！</span></span>就是那种无脑的<span><span>、</span></span>听话的小跟班<span><span>，</span></span>这样做什么事情才不容易被发现不是吗<span><span>？</span></span>况且叶万山还是军部的<span><span>，</span></span>怎么看怎么适合利用啊<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>你们说<span><span>，</span></span>今天发生的这些值不值得纪念呢<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p><strong>6</strong></p>
 <p>在聚会上答应了叶轻舟要教她<span><span>，</span></span>我自然也不能只是说说<span><span>，</span></span>毕竟以后还要利用人家<span><span>。</span></span>所以我就带着叶轻舟一起<span><span>，</span></span>从瑜伽塑形<span><span>，</span></span>再到造型设计<span><span>、</span></span>衣着搭配等等<span><span>，</span></span>最后是我们何家的那一套小到微笑的规矩<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>叶轻舟倒是学得认真<span><span>，</span></span>但不过是学个表面罢了<span><span>，</span></span>像我这种何家养出来的女儿从小耳濡目染<span><span>，</span></span>怎么做个端庄大方的优秀女人是骨子里刻着的<span><span>。</span></span>怎么可能让旁人轻轻松松学走<span><span>？</span></span>不然还怎么彰显我恶毒女配的优势呢<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>再说了<span><span>，</span></span>我本来的目的也不是这么简单啊<span><span>，</span></span>利用叶轻舟办事才是最重要的<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这次我决定了<span><span>，</span></span>不能正面对男主和女主下手<span><span>，</span></span>太傻了<span><span>，</span></span>要走迂回战术<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我记得女主是个心理医生来着<span><span>，</span></span>有个自己的心理诊疗所<span><span>。</span></span>打听到今天女主不在诊疗所<span><span>，</span></span>我就带着叶轻舟<span><span>「</span></span>浩浩荡荡<span><span>」</span></span>地去了……砸店<span><span>？</span></span>呵<span><span>，</span></span>这么 low 的手段<span><span>，</span></span>我都不屑用<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>我们今天去学什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟在车里好奇地看着车窗外陌生的街景<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你先说说<span><span>，</span></span>你这几天跟着我都学了点什么吧<span><span>，</span></span>我听听成果<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我看看叶轻舟<span><span>，</span></span>叶轻舟有点不好意思地笑笑<span><span>，</span></span>抓了抓裙子<span><span>，</span></span>耸耸肩<span><span>，</span></span>说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>说实话<span><span>，</span></span>我可能要辜负你一片好心了<span><span>，</span></span>我比较笨<span><span>，</span></span>好像……好像……<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶轻舟就像一个做了错事不敢面对家长的孩子一样<span><span>，</span></span>把头轻轻低了下去<span><span>。</span></span>我安慰地理了理她的头发<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>没事<span><span>，</span></span>什么事都不是一蹴而就的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶轻舟突然抬起头<span><span>，</span></span>眼睛亮晶晶的看着我<span><span>，</span></span>一扫低落<span><span>，</span></span>语气欢悦地说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>但我喜欢跟何茵姐在一起<span><span>，</span></span>就好像离自己的梦想更进一步了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我一下子愣住了<span><span>，</span></span>我没有想到这个小姑娘这么认真<span><span>，</span></span>我有些愧疚地说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>如果我没你想象中的那么好<span><span>、</span></span>那么完美呢<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>没关系的<span><span>，</span></span>在我眼里何茵姐就是最完美的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟脱口而出<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我没好意思再看着叶轻舟<span><span>，</span></span>把脸别开<span><span>，</span></span>小声地念了一声<span><span>「</span></span>傻孩子……<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>到了祝姣的心理诊疗所<span><span>，</span></span>我带着叶轻舟下了车<span><span>。</span></span>叶轻舟看了一眼招牌<span><span>，</span></span>不解地问<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>这是家心理诊疗所吧<span><span>，</span></span>我们来这里干什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我眼都不带眨一下地背着我为叶轻舟准备好的剧本<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>哦<span><span>，</span></span>这不是订婚日期快到了吗<span><span>，</span></span>琐碎的事宜太多了<span><span>，</span></span>我最近有点焦虑<span><span>，</span></span>睡也睡不好<span><span>，</span></span>就想跟心理医生聊聊<span><span>，</span></span>看看会不会有效果<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>说着我还指着我今天早上画了好久的淡淡的黑眼圈给叶轻舟看<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>瞧<span><span>，</span></span>都用了好多次眼霜了<span><span>，</span></span>也没淡多少<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶轻舟看着我的黑眼圈<span><span>，</span></span>担忧地叫了一声<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>呀<span><span>！</span></span>这么严重吗<span><span>？</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>你不要紧吧<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>没事<span><span>，</span></span>没事<span><span>，</span></span>你先陪我进去吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我拉住了叶轻舟的手<span><span>，</span></span>往里走<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>叶轻舟很自然地挽住了我<span><span>，</span></span>还小声跟我说着<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>我跟你说<span><span>，</span></span>我知道……对睡眠很有帮助的<span><span>，</span></span>实在不行你就……也是帮助睡眠的<span><span>！</span></span>牛奶也很有用……<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我的心里一暖<span><span>，</span></span>真好的小姑娘<span><span>，</span></span>希望以后她还能像现在一样崇拜我<span><span>，</span></span>真心对我好<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我走进诊疗所<span><span>，</span></span>里面的工作人员就好像认识我一样<span><span>，</span></span>很亲切地走上来问<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何小姐您又来了<span><span>，</span></span>今天怎么没预约啊<span><span>？</span></span>祝老师今天出去了不在呢<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>就是女主不在我才来啊<span><span>！</span></span>在的时候来这干嘛<span><span>？</span></span>吵架吗<span><span>？</span></span>不过这个接待为什么认识我啊<span><span>？</span></span>我以前来过吗<span><span>？</span></span>还是我太出名了而她又恰好是天生自来熟<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>我也佯作熟稔地打着哈哈<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>哦<span><span>，</span></span>今天也不是什么严重的问题<span><span>，</span></span>就是想找个人聊聊<span><span>，</span></span>不用她也行<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>工作人员又问<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>怎么<span><span>？</span></span>是之前的问题又犯了吗<span><span>？</span></span>影响大吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>你以前也有这种情况吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟问我<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我哪知道啊<span><span>？</span></span>我不记得我有什么问题啊<span><span>！</span></span>这也不在我的剧本里啊<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>我没办法<span><span>，</span></span>只能绕着圈子地说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>没事了已经<span><span>，</span></span>今天就是睡眠不好<span><span>，</span></span>劳烦你给我安排个老师就行<span><span>，</span></span>不是什么大问题的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哦哦哦<span><span>，</span></span>原来是这样啊<span><span>！</span></span>好的<span><span>，</span></span>那您稍等<span><span>，</span></span>我去给您安排老师<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我赶忙笑着点头<span><span>，</span></span>终于打发走了<span><span>。</span></span>但是这突然让我感觉自己好像丢了一段时间的记忆<span><span>。</span></span>我又想起来那天聚会上有人说我两个月前出过车祸<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>还没等我自己想明白<span><span>，</span></span>那人又回来了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何小姐<span><span>，</span></span>已经帮您安排好了<span><span>，</span></span>老师已经在您的包间里面了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>说着工作人员又看了看叶轻舟对我说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那我就先安排您的朋友去休息区了<span><span>。</span></span>希望本次咨询能有助何小姐睡眠<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>然后就带着叶轻舟走了<span><span>，</span></span>留下了一脸懵逼的我……我的包间<span><span>？</span></span>excuse me<span><span>？</span></span>我并没有印象我的包间是哪个房间啊<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>我犹豫地站了起来<span><span>，</span></span>却又不能表现出我的疑惑<span><span>，</span></span>我就凭着感觉走<span><span>。</span></span>身旁走过几个其他工作人员<span><span>，</span></span>她们也热情地跟我打着招呼<span><span>，</span></span>叫着<span><span>「</span></span>何小姐<span><span>」</span></span><span><span>，</span></span>就好像我是他们的常客一样<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我站定在一个房间前<span><span>，</span></span>犹豫不决地小心地敲了敲门<span><span>。</span></span>我也不知道为什么我会来到这个房间<span><span>，</span></span>但是就是毫无缘由地觉得就应该是这一间<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>果然<span><span>，</span></span>敲门声刚落<span><span>，</span></span>屋内传来一个声音<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>是何小姐吗<span><span>？</span></span>请进<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我推开门走进去<span><span>，</span></span>心理医生是一个四五十岁的女人<span><span>，</span></span>她站在茶水台泡着茶叶<span><span>，</span></span>我就径直走向了窗子下面那个长沙发<span><span>，</span></span>躺了下来<span><span>。</span></span>我都安排好了<span><span>，</span></span>我只用做做样子就可以了<span><span>，</span></span>之后再假装精神崩溃<span><span>，</span></span>医院那边开个证明就行了<span><span>，</span></span>到时候有叶轻舟给我作证<span><span>，</span></span>祝姣这家心理诊疗所就可以停业几天了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>而霸道总裁一般都不喜欢自己的女人在外面有自己的事业<span><span>，</span></span>所以这种小事厉绍也估计不会上心<span><span>。</span></span>以叶轻舟的性格<span><span>，</span></span>一定不放心我<span><span>，</span></span>这样她就会去找这种情况的解决方法<span><span>，</span></span>到时候难免挖掘其他出现问题的患者<span><span>，</span></span>当然<span><span>，</span></span>这些患者我都安排好了<span><span>。</span></span>这些足以让祝姣在心理治疗方面身败名裂<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>不用担心会被厉绍发现<span><span>，</span></span>呵<span><span>，</span></span>心理治疗这种事会出现什么效果心理医生也不好说吧<span><span>！</span></span>而且患者是叶轻舟找的<span><span>，</span></span>我又是受害者<span><span>，</span></span>这次怎么也没证据说是我吧<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>我闭上眼睛<span><span>，</span></span>听见有茶盘放在桌面的声音<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何小姐怎么还是这么着急啊<span><span>？</span></span>今天又要回公司处理哪个合同啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>心理医生打趣道<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>合同是双方的<span><span>，</span></span>健康才是自己的不是吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我听着心理医生一副<span><span>「</span></span>我们很熟<span><span>」</span></span>的语气<span><span>，</span></span>不知道为什么<span><span>，</span></span>有点不安<span><span>，</span></span>就好像我失去了一部分很重要<span><span>、</span></span>很关键的东西<span><span>。</span></span>我没有睁开眼<span><span>，</span></span>只是下意识伸手<span><span>，</span></span>就抓住了一个小茶杯<span><span>，</span></span>然后另一只手摸索着按下了一个键<span><span>，</span></span>沙发就开始上升<span><span>，</span></span>等到了一个舒适的角度<span><span>，</span></span>我松开了手<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这一系列动作就好像我做了无数次一样<span><span>，</span></span>我甚至不用睁眼就可以完成<span><span>！</span></span>这是怎么回事<span><span>？</span></span>我强按下心里的疑惑<span><span>，</span></span>装作若无其事地准备喝茶<span><span>，</span></span>刚放在嘴旁<span><span>，</span></span>生生停住了接下来的动作<span><span>，</span></span>身体都僵硬了几秒<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这……这茶叶是……是我们何家自制的<span><span>！</span></span>是我爷爷在自家的茶园种的<span><span>，</span></span>亲自炒的<span><span>！</span></span>因为爷爷总想何家的小辈们忆苦思甜<span><span>，</span></span>特意将茶叶炒得狠了<span><span>，</span></span>因此闻起来会有丝丝的焦苦味<span><span>，</span></span>但是……我小小地啄了一口<span><span>，</span></span>没错<span><span>！</span></span>但是喝起来会有很强的回甘<span><span>！</span></span>这种茶爷爷只做了两回<span><span>，</span></span>分给我<span><span>、</span></span>何树<span><span>，</span></span>以及叔叔伯伯家的表亲小辈们<span><span>，</span></span>属于何家的内部茶<span><span>，</span></span>祝姣的小诊疗所怎么会有的<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>有一种不好的念头油然而生<span><span>：</span></span>难道我之前真的有什么心理问题来找过祝姣<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>我没敢开口问<span><span>，</span></span>就这么躺着让心理医生为我做完了心理指导<span><span>。</span></span>即使我真的来找过祝姣也不能阻止我这个计划的进行<span><span>，</span></span>剧本已经写好了<span><span>，</span></span>我这个主演怎么也不能罢演啊<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>我起身谢过心理医生<span><span>，</span></span>心理医生也祝我健康<span><span>，</span></span>然后我推开门<span><span>，</span></span>立马换上一副精神虚弱的样子<span><span>，</span></span>微微皱着眉<span><span>。</span></span>看见叶轻舟在外面<span><span>，</span></span>我假装强颜欢笑地打起精神去拉着叶轻舟的手臂<span><span>，</span></span>装着轻松地说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>好很多了<span><span>，</span></span>轻舟<span><span>，</span></span>我们走吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶轻舟的反应也没让我失望<span><span>，</span></span>她担忧地看着我的脸色<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>你真的好点了吗<span><span>？</span></span>怎么感觉脸色更差了呢<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我倒是不在意地摆摆手<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>心理治疗嘛<span><span>，</span></span>什么结果心理医生也说不好的<span><span>，</span></span>走吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>一切都在按着我的剧本发展着<span><span>，</span></span>叶轻舟不放心我一个人在我的公寓<span><span>，</span></span>而我又因为工作回何家不方便<span><span>。</span></span>叶轻舟主动提出来在公寓陪我<span><span>，</span></span>我答应了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>到了晚上<span><span>，</span></span>叶轻舟为我准备了牛奶<span><span>，</span></span>我喝下后表示我已经好很多了<span><span>，</span></span>八点多<span><span>，</span></span>就进了房间要休息<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>别急<span><span>，</span></span>我的表演要开始了……到了十点<span><span>，</span></span>我突然摔碎了玻璃杯<span><span>，</span></span>听见叶轻舟着急的脚步声<span><span>，</span></span>我一笑<span><span>，</span></span>然后突然抓乱自己的头发<span><span>，</span></span>整个身体都开始颤抖<span><span>，</span></span>情绪也很激动<span><span>，</span></span>整个人都很焦急<span><span>，</span></span>嘴里还不停念叨着<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>厉绍<span><span>，</span></span>厉绍<span><span>，</span></span>你应该娶我的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不要……不要……不要去监狱<span><span>，</span></span>不要把我留在这<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>啊啊啊<span><span>，</span></span>祝姣<span><span>，</span></span>都是你<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>…….</p>
 <p>说着我还开始流眼泪<span><span>，</span></span>开始推倒椅子<span><span>，</span></span>然后疯狂地翻我的柜子<span><span>、</span></span>抽屉<span><span>，</span></span>好像在找什么<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>叶轻舟推开房门看着疯狂的我都愣住了<span><span>，</span></span>我抓着自己的头发<span><span>，</span></span>又狠狠地敲着自己的头<span><span>，</span></span>叶轻舟赶快冲上来抓住我的手<span><span>，</span></span>着急地说着<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>不要不要<span><span>，</span></span>不要这样<span><span>，</span></span>不要伤害自己<span><span>，</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>醒醒<span><span>，</span></span>冷静冷静<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>也许是没遇见过这样的情况<span><span>，</span></span>又或者是没见过这个与平常冷静大方的何茵不同的样子<span><span>，</span></span>叶轻舟除了抓着我的手安慰我<span><span>，</span></span>让我冷静外<span><span>。</span></span>别的她什么也没做<span><span>，</span></span>也是<span><span>，</span></span>她也不知道怎么做<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>其实我也没见过自己这个样子<span><span>，</span></span>但是不知道为什么<span><span>，</span></span>这样癫狂的自己我竟觉得有些熟悉<span><span>，</span></span>有些……有些理所应当<span><span>，</span></span>就好像我就是这样的一样<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>为了增强喜剧效果<span><span>，</span></span>加重事态的严重性<span><span>，</span></span>我想到了安眠药<span><span>，</span></span>但是我家应该没有这种东西吧<span><span>？</span></span>失算了<span><span>，</span></span>我应该买点安眠药回来的<span><span>，</span></span>这样可能会更真实点<span><span>。</span></span>一个有精神问题的人怎么能没有安眠药呢<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>索性<span><span>，</span></span>我大口喘着气<span><span>，</span></span>断断续续地念着<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>药……药……我的药呢<span><span>？</span></span>安眠药<span><span>，</span></span>我需要安眠药<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶轻舟一个什么都没遭遇过的小姑娘在这种情况下只能顺着我的话<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>好好好<span><span>，</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>你先冷静冷静<span><span>，</span></span>我马上去买安眠药<span><span>，</span></span>很快<span><span>，</span></span>你等我<span><span>，</span></span>好不好<span><span>，</span></span>很快<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶轻舟话音刚落<span><span>，</span></span>就赶忙起身<span><span>，</span></span>穿着我的睡衣就想往外跑<span><span>。</span></span>而我则不知道怎么回事<span><span>，</span></span>居然站了起来<span><span>，</span></span>抓住她的手臂<span><span>，</span></span>突然又很冷静地说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>帮我倒杯水吧<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶轻舟愣了愣<span><span>，</span></span>点点头<span><span>，</span></span>跑到厨房去倒水<span><span>。</span></span>而我就像中了邪一样<span><span>，</span></span>走到客厅的一个柜子前<span><span>，</span></span>拉开第二个抽屉<span><span>，</span></span>里面赫然摆了一抽屉的阿普挫仑<span><span>（</span></span>安眠药<span><span>）</span></span><span><span>，</span></span>连我自己都被震惊到了<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>这……这还是我的公寓吗<span><span>？</span></span>为什么<span><span>？</span></span>为什么我感觉这么陌生<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>我颤颤巍巍地伸向那些安眠药<span><span>，</span></span>鬼使神差地打开一瓶开始往嘴里倒<span><span>，</span></span>而叶轻舟刚好端着水出来<span><span>，</span></span>看到这一幕<span><span>，</span></span>吓了一跳<span><span>。</span></span>扔下杯子就冲过来阻止我<span><span>，</span></span>我感受着满嘴的药片<span><span>，</span></span>理智就好像断了一样<span><span>，</span></span>完全不知道自己在干什么<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>当我再次有意识的时候我已经在医院了<span><span>，</span></span>我晃了晃头<span><span>，</span></span>看着眼前的一片白色事物<span><span>，</span></span>终于感受到了自己的头在痛<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>说实话我没想到我会真的吃安眠药<span><span>，</span></span>我真的不知道自己发生了什么<span><span>。</span></span>可能是听到了什么动静<span><span>，</span></span>病房门突然开了<span><span>，</span></span>何树顶着两个黑眼圈进来了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>姐<span><span>，</span></span>你醒了<span><span>。</span></span>饿吗<span><span>？</span></span>喝点粥吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>何树转身拎起来一个保温桶进了病房<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我点了点头<span><span>，</span></span>冲他笑了笑<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>好<span><span>，</span></span>是有点饿了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>何树看我反应还算正常<span><span>，</span></span>松了一口气<span><span>，</span></span>坐了下来<span><span>，</span></span>为我盛了一碗粥<span><span>，</span></span>递给我<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>洗了胃<span><span>，</span></span>还睡了两天<span><span>，</span></span>怎么可能不饿<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我接过粥<span><span>，</span></span>疑惑地问何树<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我……我到底是怎么了<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>没什么大事<span><span>，</span></span>喝粥吧<span><span>，</span></span>不是饿了吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我坚持地问<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我到底怎么了<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>何树亲昵地理了理我的头发<span><span>，</span></span>岔开了话题<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我姐就是好看<span><span>，</span></span>哪怕刚睡醒也这么动人<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我拍开他的手<span><span>，</span></span>无奈地说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>别跟我来这一套<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>何树没再说话<span><span>，</span></span>笑了笑就这么静静地看着我喝粥<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>没喝两口<span><span>，</span></span>医生敲了敲门<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>病人醒了吗<span><span>？</span></span>家属出来一下吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>好<span><span>」</span></span>何树应声起身<span><span>，</span></span>为我掖了掖被角出去了<span><span>。</span></span>我隐隐约约地听见何树问了句<span><span>「</span></span>严重吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我好奇<span><span>，</span></span>就掀开被子下了床<span><span>，</span></span>何树没关门<span><span>，</span></span>我趴在门缝听着何树和医生的谈话<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>病人情况很复杂<span><span>，</span></span>精神状态很差<span><span>，</span></span>有点精神分裂<span><span>，</span></span>还有点精神衰弱<span><span>，</span></span>我们判断病人还有点焦躁症<span><span>，</span></span>可能还有……<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>后面的话就听不清了<span><span>，</span></span>和我的剧本安排一样<span><span>，</span></span>一步步都是我理想的样子<span><span>，</span></span>我就是有一点担心……我担心……担心……我不会真的有问题吧<span><span>！</span></span>这个医生不是我当时安排的那个啊<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><strong>7</strong></p>
 <p>经过上次的事件<span><span>，</span></span>何树不放心我自己住了<span><span>，</span></span>非要和我一起住照顾我<span><span>。</span></span>行吧<span><span>，</span></span>反正房子那么大<span><span>，</span></span>让给我弟住点也没什么<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>而且那天晚上我的精神很奇怪<span><span>，</span></span>做什么事都好像是不由自主的<span><span>，</span></span>我自己也有点担心<span><span>，</span></span>有个人看着我也好<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>今天<span><span>，</span></span>何树为了找到我突然精神崩溃的原因找来了叶轻舟……</p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>叶小姐你好<span><span>，</span></span>请坐<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>何树绅士地为叶轻舟拉开椅子<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>没错<span><span>，</span></span>何树和叶轻舟约在了一个餐厅里<span><span>。</span></span>何树说除了询问<span><span>，</span></span>更多的是感谢<span><span>，</span></span>感谢叶轻舟送我去医院<span><span>，</span></span>算是救了我一次<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>但是……你们两个有问题要谈拉着我干什么<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span>我一个继承巨大家产的人是很忙的好吗<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>叶轻舟红着脸坐下了<span><span>，</span></span>我看着眼前这两个人……怕不是有故事吧<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>何树刚回到位置坐下<span><span>，</span></span>叶轻舟想起什么似的<span><span>，</span></span>着急问<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>我哥开车送我来的<span><span>，</span></span>你们介不介意加个位置<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>哦嚯嚯<span><span>，</span></span>当然不介意啊<span><span>！</span></span>这样也省得我想办法去教唆叶轻舟去利用叶万山了<span><span>，</span></span>人家直接到了<span><span>，</span></span>看来今天又是我的 show time<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我笑着点点头<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>当然不介意啊<span><span>，</span></span>想来也应该是不放心你<span><span>，</span></span>一起上来吃个饭也好啊<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶轻舟看我同意了<span><span>，</span></span>激动地点点头<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我这就叫我哥上来<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>果然没一会<span><span>，</span></span>包间门口就传来了皮鞋踏地的声音<span><span>，</span></span>随后<span><span>，</span></span>包间门就被推开了<span><span>。</span></span>我们一齐向门口望去<span><span>，</span></span>叶万山今天穿了一身黑色西装<span><span>，</span></span>感觉整个人都突然正式了起来<span><span>，</span></span>颇有一股霸道总裁的气息<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>打扰了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶万山向我点了一下头<span><span>，</span></span>走到席间拉开了椅子坐下<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我就这么一直看着他走过来<span><span>，</span></span>坐下<span><span>，</span></span>才笑着点点头回应<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>应该的<span><span>，</span></span>劳烦叶先生跑一趟<span><span>，</span></span>吃个饭是应该的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我看着何树<span><span>，</span></span>他看见我看向他了<span><span>，</span></span>赶忙转开头<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>？</span></span><span><span>？</span></span><span><span>？</span></span>我弟刚刚一直在看我吗<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>小树<span><span>，</span></span>可以上菜了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我温声提醒<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>何树没看我<span><span>，</span></span>点点头<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>waiter<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何小姐看起来恢复得不错<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶万山看着我<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我点点头<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>多谢关心<span><span>，</span></span>本来也不是什么大病<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>是吗<span><span>？</span></span>我听轻舟描述挺严重的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>说着<span><span>，</span></span>叶万山转头看了一眼身旁的叶轻舟<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>叶轻舟拍了一下叶万山<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你问人家<span><span>，</span></span>人家当然说没事啊<span><span>！</span></span>我可是你妹妹<span><span>，</span></span>你要相信我<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我忍不住笑了一下<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>是真的没什么事了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那何茵姐你……就是你一个人在公寓……真的没事吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟有些担忧地问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>小树和我一起的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我看了一眼何树<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>是吧<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>何树好像有点不开心<span><span>，</span></span>点点头<span><span>，</span></span>岔开了话题<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我今天请叶小姐吃饭除了感谢以外<span><span>，</span></span>还有一件事<span><span>，</span></span>就是想拜托叶小姐回忆一下我姐出事前都有什么不正常的地方<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>何树顿了一下<span><span>，</span></span>突然语气都严肃了起来<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>医生的意思是<span><span>，</span></span>我姐虽然心理压力很大<span><span>，</span></span>但是自制力也挺强的<span><span>，</span></span>没有什么诱因是不会出现这样的事情的<span><span>。</span></span>还请叶小姐仔细回忆一下<span><span>，</span></span>有劳<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>nice<span><span>，</span></span>剧情终于走入正轨<span><span>，</span></span>真的是一步步都跟我计划的相吻合<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我拍了拍何树的胳膊<span><span>，</span></span>有些责怪地说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>小树<span><span>，</span></span>别吓到轻舟了<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶万山听后也皱起了眉头<span><span>，</span></span>但是却没有开口<span><span>。</span></span>叶轻舟将我们那天的行程一丝不差地说了一遍<span><span>，</span></span>最后义愤填膺地拍了一下桌子<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>肯定是那个诊疗所闹的<span><span>，</span></span>黑诊所<span><span>，</span></span>我和何茵姐进去的时候何茵姐还有说有笑的<span><span>，</span></span>结束了何茵姐脸色都不好了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
