 <p>我没有说话<span><span>，</span></span>喝了口水<span><span>，</span></span>打量着桌上的人的反应<span><span>。</span></span>叶轻舟正情绪激昂地说着那家诊疗所<span><span>，</span></span>何树认真地听着<span><span>，</span></span>表面没什么反应<span><span>，</span></span>但是桌下放在腿上的手都握紧了<span><span>，</span></span>而叶万山嘛……我有点看不透<span><span>，</span></span>他很若无其事地喝着水<span><span>，</span></span>还帮叶轻舟倒了一杯<span><span>，</span></span>提醒叶轻舟润润嘴<span><span>，</span></span>就好像与他没什么关系的样子<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>好吧<span><span>，</span></span>确实和他也没什么关系<span><span>。</span></span>叶万山这个态度又让我不禁怀疑叶轻舟到底能不能驱使得动叶万山啊<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>服务员的敲门声打破了包间奇奇怪怪的局面<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何总<span><span>，</span></span>菜品已经准备好了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我点点头<span><span>，</span></span>何树冲着门口说了声<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>请进<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>服务员依次进来<span><span>，</span></span>我笑着看向叶轻舟<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>先吃饭吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>何树站起来为我布着菜<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>姐<span><span>，</span></span>这些都是安神的<span><span>，</span></span>你先尝尝<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>好<span><span>，</span></span>你也吃吧<span><span>，</span></span>我记下了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我拿起筷子<span><span>，</span></span>对叶万山和叶轻舟说着<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>请<span><span>，</span></span>轻舟和叶先生不用客气的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶万山没什么动作<span><span>，</span></span>但是叶轻舟摆摆手<span><span>，</span></span>说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不行不行<span><span>，</span></span>我越想那个诊疗所越有问题<span><span>！</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>你怎么还能安心吃饭呢<span><span>？</span></span>万一他们是故意想害你呢<span><span>！</span></span>我跟你说……<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我用公筷夹了一片鱼送到叶轻舟嘴边<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>尝尝<span><span>？</span></span>他们家鱼做得挺好的<span><span>，</span></span>没有刺<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶轻舟不情不愿地闭上了嘴<span><span>，</span></span>端起来碗接过鱼片<span><span>，</span></span>又不甘心<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何茵姐……<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不用说了<span><span>」</span></span>我打断叶轻舟的话<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>这家诊疗所我很熟悉的<span><span>，</span></span>没问题的<span><span>，</span></span>应该是我自己的问题<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我又转头看向何树<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>小树<span><span>，</span></span>你也别想太多了<span><span>，</span></span>可能真的是我自己压力大了呢<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>厉绍那个混蛋<span><span>，</span></span>明明订婚是两个人的事<span><span>，</span></span>怎么能……<span><span>」</span></span>何树将筷子拍在桌子上<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>咳咳<span><span>」</span></span>我转过头假咳了两声<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>注意点<span><span>，</span></span>别忘了爸爸怎么教的<span><span>，</span></span>别没规没矩的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我又笑着向叶万山点头<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>见笑了<span><span>，</span></span>叶先生请用菜<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>虽然不知道叶万山现在对我是什么态度<span><span>，</span></span>但是我的理想目的已经达到了<span><span>，</span></span>这顿饭我吃得十分惬意<span><span>，</span></span>要不是怕人设崩塌<span><span>，</span></span>我都想加碗饭了<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>饭后<span><span>，</span></span>餐厅楼下要分别了<span><span>，</span></span>叶轻舟不舍地拉着我的手说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>哥哥说何茵姐你需要休息<span><span>，</span></span>这段时间就不允许我去找你了<span><span>，</span></span>何茵姐你要好好休息<span><span>，</span></span>等你好了我再去找你玩<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>好<span><span>，</span></span>你在家也要听你哥哥的话<span><span>，</span></span>别乱跑<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我拍了拍叶轻舟的手<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>然后松开叶轻舟的手准备上车<span><span>，</span></span>叶轻舟突然愤愤地说着<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>你放心<span><span>，</span></span>我也不会闲着<span><span>，</span></span>肯定要把你发病的事弄清楚<span><span>，</span></span>那个诊疗所我不会放过的<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我摇摇头<span><span>，</span></span>笑而不语<span><span>，</span></span>没看叶轻舟<span><span>，</span></span>反而看向叶万山<span><span>，</span></span>叶万山也看着我<span><span>，</span></span>我冲他点点头<span><span>，</span></span>他也对我点点头<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>然后我就上车离去了<span><span>。</span></span>我只不过礼貌地冲叶万山点点头<span><span>，</span></span>表示告别<span><span>，</span></span>怎么他回我一个这么高深的呢<span><span>？</span></span>好复杂啊<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><strong>8</strong></p>
 <p>事情在如期发展着<span><span>，</span></span>据我安排的人向我反映<span><span>，</span></span>果真有人在调查祝姣的诊疗所<span><span>，</span></span>一切都不用我动手<span><span>，</span></span>而矛头却都指向了祝姣<span><span>，</span></span>真好……</p>
 <p>本来我的房子那么大<span><span>，</span></span>分一间给我弟弟住也没什么<span><span>，</span></span>但是……但是这几天发生的事情让我很迷茫……</p>
 <p>何树来的第一天<span><span>，</span></span>我和往常一样起床下楼<span><span>，</span></span>刚下到楼梯口就看见何树已经坐在沙发上看早间新闻了<span><span>，</span></span>何树看见我下楼了<span><span>，</span></span>就站了起来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>何树笑着跟我打招呼<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>姐<span><span>，</span></span>早啊<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>本来这也没什么<span><span>，</span></span>但是当我看着何树穿着一个宽宽的白 T 恤<span><span>，</span></span>和一个大裤衩露着两条又白又直的腿的时候……我突然冒出来一个想法<span><span>，</span></span>我觉得他在色诱我<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>我感觉我脑子有问题了<span><span>，</span></span>但是我也不知道怎么了<span><span>，</span></span>我就开口了<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>光着腿不冷吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>何树看了看我<span><span>，</span></span>反问<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那姐你冷吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我看了一眼自己<span><span>，</span></span>我穿着吊肩的真丝睡裙<span><span>，</span></span>比起来我睡裙的布还不一定有何树那一身多……</p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>呵呵<span><span>，</span></span>我……我……咱俩能一样吗<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我讪笑着赶紧回卧室换衣服<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>然后我就终于意识到了<span><span>，</span></span>我的公寓多了一个人<span><span>，</span></span>还是多了一个男人……</p>
 <p>洗漱过后<span><span>，</span></span>我走到厨房准备倒杯牛奶<span><span>，</span></span>烤个面包<span><span>，</span></span>可是何树却先我一步拉开了厨房的门<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我熬了小米粥<span><span>，</span></span>姐姐经常忘记吃饭<span><span>，</span></span>小米粥养胃<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我愣住了<span><span>，</span></span>我弟弟这么懂我的吗<span><span>？</span></span>哦嚯嚯<span><span>，</span></span>房间没白给他住哦<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>我点点头<span><span>，</span></span>理所应当地在餐厅坐下了<span><span>，</span></span>等着何树的小米粥<span><span>，</span></span>何树在厨房用面包机烤了面包<span><span>，</span></span>一齐端了出来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>久等了<span><span>，</span></span>my queen<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>何树放下一碗还冒着热气的小米粥<span><span>，</span></span>和两片微微焦的面包片<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我记得你喜欢焦一点的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>嗯<span><span>」</span></span>我点点头<span><span>，</span></span>这个弟弟上道<span><span>，</span></span>给赞<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>吃了何树的爱心早餐<span><span>，</span></span>我就去了公司<span><span>，</span></span>其实也就是日常打卡<span><span>，</span></span>就医生给我那个诊断书<span><span>，</span></span>一时半会儿谁敢让我工作啊<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>坐到下午下班<span><span>，</span></span>我回到公寓<span><span>，</span></span>何树又给了我一个惊喜<span><span>，</span></span>我简直太吃这一套了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我刚一开门<span><span>，</span></span>还没来得及换鞋<span><span>，</span></span>就看见何树围着围裙从厨房端着菜出来了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>看来你的小秘没骗我<span><span>，</span></span>时间一点都不差<span><span>，</span></span>快洗手来吃饭<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>何树放下菜<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我也是惊呆了<span><span>，</span></span>还以为我要和何树纠结晚上点什么外卖呢<span><span>！</span></span>没想到我弟弟这么贤惠<span><span>，</span></span>都把我安排得明明白白了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我收拾好坐下了<span><span>，</span></span>很好<span><span>，</span></span>三菜一汤<span><span>，</span></span>太贤惠了<span><span>，</span></span>我都忍不住想流泪<span><span>，</span></span>何树<span><span>，</span></span>收拾收拾出嫁吧<span><span>！</span></span>你比我像个女人<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>吃着饭<span><span>，</span></span>何树突然问我<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>姐<span><span>，</span></span>你中午一般是不是不回家啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>怎么这么问<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我喝了一口汤<span><span>，</span></span>抿抿嘴<span><span>，</span></span>美味<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哦<span><span>，</span></span>也没什么<span><span>，</span></span>就是我中午做了菜等你回来呢<span><span>，</span></span>结果发现你不回家<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>不知道是故意的还是我的错觉<span><span>，</span></span>我感觉何树的语气哀怨<span><span>，</span></span>但是面色如常<span><span>，</span></span>非常有一种小怨妇的气质<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>老弟<span><span>，</span></span>我哪知道你有这个手艺<span><span>！</span></span>你早说啊<span><span>，</span></span>以后我天天回家<span><span>，</span></span>员工餐厅是真的太不合我胃口了<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>也不是<span><span>，</span></span>就是今天中午比较忙而已<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我一本正经地撒着谎<span><span>，</span></span>脸都不带红的<span><span>，</span></span>夹菜的手也很稳<span><span>，</span></span>我上辈子一定是个演员<span><span>，</span></span>拿过奥斯卡小金人的那种<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>饭后<span><span>，</span></span>何树把碗筷放进洗碗机<span><span>，</span></span>我觉得无聊<span><span>，</span></span>就干脆拉着他去我公寓的负一层<span><span>，</span></span>其实也不算负一层<span><span>，</span></span>就是错了半层<span><span>，</span></span>刚好有个小空间<span><span>，</span></span>我当时脑子一热就弄成了个小的放映室<span><span>，</span></span>后来还嫌没什么用<span><span>，</span></span>现在想想还不错<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我盘腿坐在沙发上<span><span>，</span></span>何树也坐了下来<span><span>，</span></span>我找了一个恐怖片<span><span>，</span></span>看着看着<span><span>，</span></span>我感觉灯亮着没什么气氛<span><span>，</span></span>就按着遥控器就把所有的灯给关了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>房间暗了下来<span><span>，</span></span>只有屏幕泛着蓝光<span><span>，</span></span>音响发出那些恐怖的音效<span><span>，</span></span>可能是下了一层更接近地面<span><span>，</span></span>我还感觉有丝丝冷意<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>就当所有恐怖气氛都渲染好<span><span>，</span></span>马上就要到关键时刻了<span><span>，</span></span>突然我感觉有一只手抓住了我的脚腕<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>我吓了一跳<span><span>，</span></span>想缩回脚但是根本收不回来<span><span>。</span></span>我感觉那个手虽然在微微颤抖<span><span>，</span></span>但却十分有力<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>然后一个小小的声音说<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>姐<span><span>，</span></span>能不能……能不能把灯打开<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>是何树<span><span>。</span></span>这让我想起来八岁那年何树被绑架过<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>说起来也是因为我<span><span>，</span></span>何树小的时候长得就清秀<span><span>，</span></span>再加上性子温和<span><span>，</span></span>七八岁的时候就跟个小女生一样<span><span>，</span></span>反倒是我大大咧咧的<span><span>，</span></span>跟个男生一样<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>八岁那年放学<span><span>，</span></span>我带着何树回家<span><span>，</span></span>觉得家和学校也不远<span><span>，</span></span>就一直没让父亲安排车接送<span><span>。</span></span>可那天<span><span>，</span></span>走到半路突然就冲出来一个摩托车<span><span>，</span></span>车后座上的人一把就抓住了何树<span><span>，</span></span>拎着小何树就开走了<span><span>，</span></span>我一点反应的时间都没<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我急急忙忙地跑回家告诉父亲<span><span>，</span></span>父亲也着急地报了警<span><span>，</span></span>警察初步断定是绑架<span><span>，</span></span>要我们回去等电话<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>果然<span><span>，</span></span>半夜<span><span>，</span></span>一个电话打到了父亲的手机上<span><span>：</span></span>你的女儿何茵在我们手上<span><span>，</span></span>我们知道你报警了<span><span>，</span></span>但是想她活命的话<span><span>，</span></span>多少钱还是要看何总的意思了……</p>
 <p>我自然是听到了电话的内容<span><span>，</span></span>父亲看看我<span><span>，</span></span>没说话<span><span>，</span></span>叹了口气跟绑匪交流着<span><span>，</span></span>挂了电话又跟警察交流<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>但是当时我的脑子都是乱的<span><span>，</span></span>父亲虽然不说<span><span>，</span></span>但是我清楚地知道<span><span>，</span></span>是何树替我遭了罪<span><span>，</span></span>这一劫<span><span>，</span></span>是我欠他的<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>后来因为电话里的声音是从不同音频里面一句句截出来的<span><span>，</span></span>又因为时间短无法定位<span><span>，</span></span>我们只能按约定的时间地点交钱<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>最后找到何树的时候是在交钱的地方<span><span>，</span></span>我们把钱用隔水纸包好扔下水<span><span>，</span></span>而何树被绑好放在一个船上的木箱子里漂下来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那个箱子里委实暗<span><span>，</span></span>一点光都不透……可能是怕何树看见什么吧……</p>
 <p>我们都不敢问何树遭遇了什么<span><span>，</span></span>何树也不哭<span><span>，</span></span>就只是说有点疲惫<span><span>，</span></span>我们把他接回家他就睡了<span><span>。</span></span>此后<span><span>，</span></span>不知什么时候何树床头多了一盏长明灯<span><span>，</span></span>就连白天都不灭……</p>
 <p>所以我现在感觉自己好像干了什么错事<span><span>，</span></span>我想把灯打开<span><span>，</span></span>何树又突然说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>没事<span><span>，</span></span>姐<span><span>，</span></span>我没事<span><span>。</span></span>你就让我拉着<span><span>，</span></span>我感觉到身边有人就没事了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我拉着何树的手把他拉到我的怀里<span><span>，</span></span>然后两条腿环住了他的腰<span><span>，</span></span>就像小时候一样<span><span>，</span></span>就这么把他抱在我的怀里<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>没事<span><span>，</span></span>姐姐在呢<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我感觉何树的身体突然僵硬了<span><span>，</span></span>然后又放松了<span><span>，</span></span>黑暗中我听到他笑了一声<span><span>，</span></span>然后紧紧地抓住了我的手臂<span><span>，</span></span>说着<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>嗯<span><span>，</span></span>姐姐在<span><span>，</span></span>我不怕<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我们就这样待着<span><span>，</span></span>谁也没有开口<span><span>，</span></span>灯也一直没有开<span><span>。</span></span>直到电影结束<span><span>，</span></span>灯自动亮了<span><span>，</span></span>我才发现何树睡着了<span><span>，</span></span>突然亮起的灯光还让他不适地皱起了眉毛<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我下意识地伸出另一只手轻轻地盖在了他的眼睛上<span><span>，</span></span>在他的耳边小声说了句<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>谢谢<span><span>，</span></span>我的小树<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>然后我也睡着了<span><span>，</span></span>等我醒过来我已经在自己的房间了<span><span>，</span></span>应该是何树把我带回来的<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>怎么办<span><span>？</span></span>我现在感觉我弟弟超贤惠<span><span>，</span></span>而且他好像还在撩我<span><span>？</span></span>但是我又没有证据<span><span>，</span></span>我该怎么办<span><span>？</span></span>在线等<span><span>，</span></span>挺急的<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><strong>9</strong></p>
 <p>我紧抓着自己睡衣的前襟<span><span>，</span></span>努力保持镇静<span><span>。</span></span>我不怕<span><span>，</span></span>我不怕<span><span>，</span></span>我不怕<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>然后小心翼翼地迈出一只脚<span><span>，</span></span>向前轻轻地放去<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>一旁的何树也小声安慰我<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>没事<span><span>，</span></span>姐<span><span>，</span></span>这只是个小场面<span><span>，</span></span>你不用紧张<span><span>。</span></span>多大的谈判<span><span>、</span></span>酒席你都面不改色地去了<span><span>，</span></span>这算什么<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我吞了吞口水<span><span>，</span></span>又将伸出去的脚快速收了回来<span><span>，</span></span>焦急地说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你个小屁孩懂什么<span><span>！</span></span>这可是生死攸关的大时刻<span><span>，</span></span>哪是那些小场面能比的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>何树无奈地瞥了我一眼<span><span>，</span></span>我又战战兢兢地试探性地迈出一只脚<span><span>，</span></span>还没放平<span><span>，</span></span>就感觉身后有一股神秘的东方力量推了我一把……</p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>姐<span><span>，</span></span>安心上秤吧<span><span>，</span></span>哪那么多话啊<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我还没来得及回头教训何树<span><span>，</span></span>就只看见面前这个<span><span>「</span></span>恶魔<span><span>」</span></span>上的指针稳稳地停在了一个数字面前<span><span>，</span></span>我直接如被雷劈过一样愣在原地……</p>
 <p>随后在我家里<span><span>，</span></span>一个杀猪般的声音响了起来<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>啊啊啊<span><span>！</span></span>我居然真的重了<span><span>！</span></span>何树都怪你<span><span>，</span></span>明天开始你收拾东西滚回何家去<span><span>！</span></span>我这标准的女神体重都没了……<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>何树满不在意地捂着耳朵转过身<span><span>，</span></span>走向厨房<span><span>，</span></span>嘴角却不经意地挂上了笑容<span><span>，</span></span>像平常一样问着<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>姐<span><span>，</span></span>中午想吃什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我愤愤地走下体重秤<span><span>，</span></span>嘴里嚷嚷着<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我跟你说<span><span>，</span></span>我一定要减肥了<span><span>，</span></span>你这次说什么都要给我走……<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>说什么都没用<span><span>，</span></span>我不会再犹豫了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我不能再给你机会了……别废话<span><span>，</span></span>你赶紧收拾东西去<span><span>」</span></span>……</p>
 <p>可听到何树问我吃什么<span><span>，</span></span>我想都没想<span><span>，</span></span>脱口而出<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>爆炒肥肠<span><span>，</span></span>奶油蘑菇汤……<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>好嘞<span><span>，</span></span>姐<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>呸<span><span>，</span></span>何茵你个没出息的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我拼命地拍着自己的嘴<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>中午正吃着饭<span><span>，</span></span>手机突然响了<span><span>，</span></span>我看了一眼手机<span><span>，</span></span>是我的小秘<span><span>。</span></span>我看了一眼何树<span><span>，</span></span>还是接了<span><span>，</span></span>我一个总裁划水这么多天<span><span>，</span></span>现在如果还不接秘书电话我自己都感觉过分了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>喂<span><span>，</span></span>小秘<span><span>，</span></span>你说……哦<span><span>，</span></span>下午有个会议对方一定要我出席是吗<span><span>？</span></span>好<span><span>，</span></span>正好我这几天休息得也差不多了<span><span>。</span></span>还有什么<span><span>，</span></span>你说就是了……<span><span>」</span></span>我还没听完我家小秘的话<span><span>，</span></span>何树就一把夺过我的手机<span><span>，</span></span>看都不看就挂掉<span><span>，</span></span>笑呵呵地对我说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>姐<span><span>，</span></span>别光教育我<span><span>，</span></span>爸还说食不言呢<span><span>，</span></span>吃饭的时候就不要工作了<span><span>，</span></span>血液被用于大脑的话对胃不好了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>what<span><span>？</span></span>还有这种说法<span><span>？</span></span>那酒桌谈生意岂不是太折寿了<span><span>？</span></span>我弟弟也不老啊<span><span>？</span></span>什么时候开始关注这种消息了<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>我点了点头<span><span>，</span></span>趁何树放松警惕<span><span>，</span></span>又一把夺过手机<span><span>，</span></span>回拨了过去<span><span>。</span></span>然后用嚣张的眼神看着何树<span><span>：</span></span>哼<span><span>，</span></span>我想怎么样就怎么样<span><span>！</span></span>你姐姐永远是你姐姐<span><span>，</span></span>别想管我<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>何树无奈地笑了笑<span><span>，</span></span>开始收拾碗筷<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>酒足饭饱<span><span>，</span></span>司机接我到了何氏<span><span>，</span></span>我踩着我的女王高度的高跟鞋<span><span>，</span></span>接受着员工们敬仰的目光<span><span>，</span></span>来到我的办公室<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>虽然下午这个项目也不小<span><span>，</span></span>但是我隐约记得两家都合作很长时间了<span><span>，</span></span>而且前几次都是双方经理签的<span><span>，</span></span>我感觉就这样的关系应该不需要高层出面吧<span><span>？</span></span>难道是出什么变故了<span><span>？</span></span>还是对面高层的小哥哥觊觎我的美貌一定要见见我<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>我怀着<span><span>「</span></span>忐忑<span><span>」</span></span>的心<span><span>，</span></span>看着小秘推开会议室的门<span><span>，</span></span>就看见会议室里只坐着一个男人……和三个女人<span><span>（</span></span>抱歉<span><span>，</span></span>我只注意有没有小哥哥了<span><span>，</span></span>没仔细看有没有小姐姐<span><span>）</span></span><span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>但是我的第二个想法却破灭了<span><span>。</span></span>因为这个男人的岁数都可以做我爸了<span><span>，</span></span>就算他对我有非分之想……不对<span><span>，</span></span>他对我连想都不能想<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我不能表露出我的失望<span><span>，</span></span>站在那里端着我何氏大小姐之端庄优雅笑……一动不动<span><span>。</span></span>因为我根本不知道这个人是谁<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>我的小秘可能是看出来了我的尴尬<span><span>，</span></span>悄悄地附在我耳边说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何总<span><span>，</span></span>这是叶家的叶总<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>哦<span><span>？</span></span>叶家的叶总<span><span>？</span></span>是我想的那个叶总吗<span><span>？</span></span>就是那个把叶万山送进军部<span><span>，</span></span>叶轻舟的父亲<span><span>？</span></span>都跟我爸平辈了还觊觎我的美貌<span><span>！</span></span>hetui<span><span>！</span></span>这个老男人<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我走上前<span><span>，</span></span>礼貌伸出手<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>叶叔叔怎么来了也不知会我一声<span><span>，</span></span>咱们找个茶馆聊啊<span><span>，</span></span>办公室多拘束<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶有钱握了一下我的手<span><span>，</span></span>松开了<span><span>，</span></span>乐呵呵地说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>嗨<span><span>，</span></span>何小姐<span><span>，</span></span>这哪能是我啊<span><span>，</span></span>还不都是我那个闺女<span><span>，</span></span>真的是又要麻烦你了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哦哦哦<span><span>，</span></span>原来是轻舟啊<span><span>。</span></span>我还以为叶叔叔要见我<span><span>，</span></span>是合作出了什么意外呢<span><span>，</span></span>吓得我赶紧赶过来和叶叔叔您商谈呢<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我就说<span><span>，</span></span>我和叶有钱有什么可聊<span><span>，</span></span>合同条款早就敲定好了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那不能<span><span>，</span></span>那不能<span><span>，</span></span>何小姐做事我放心的<span><span>。</span></span>我闭着眼都敢跟何小姐合作<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶有钱不知道为什么<span><span>，</span></span>突然很急切地解释<span><span>，</span></span>生怕我误会的样子<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>不过也正好<span><span>，</span></span>确实是挺久没见了<span><span>，</span></span>看看这个叶轻舟的办事效率怎么样<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>叶叔叔谬赞了<span><span>，</span></span>那……轻舟……<span><span>」</span></span>我话还没说完<span><span>，</span></span>就感觉一个人从后面扑到了我的背上<span><span>，</span></span>然后我的眼前就一片黑暗了<span><span>，</span></span>一个奇奇怪怪的声音从背后响起<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>猜猜我是谁<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>还能有谁这么无聊啊<span><span>！</span></span>我无奈地摇摇头<span><span>，</span></span>还没开口<span><span>，</span></span>就只听叶有钱呵斥道<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>轻舟<span><span>，</span></span>这是何小姐<span><span>，</span></span>别没大没小的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>然后我就感觉眼前亮了起来<span><span>，</span></span>叶轻舟很不情愿地放下了手<span><span>，</span></span>撒娇地叫着<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>爸<span><span>，</span></span>我和何茵姐关系很好的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我点头附和<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>叶叔叔<span><span>，</span></span>轻舟就像我妹妹一样<span><span>，</span></span>没事的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那也不行<span><span>」</span></span><span><span>，</span></span>叶有钱走过来拉着叶轻舟走到我对面站好<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>以后要对何小姐尊敬点<span><span>，</span></span>在何小姐身边注意点<span><span>，</span></span>别再毛毛躁躁的跟个疯子似的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我越来越有点看不太明白这个叶有钱了<span><span>。</span></span>不知道为什么<span><span>，</span></span>我总觉得叶有钱对我客气过度了<span><span>。</span></span>他明明是我的长辈<span><span>，</span></span>这一口一个的<span><span>「</span></span>何小姐<span><span>」</span></span>给我一种叶有钱对我很恭敬的感觉<span><span>，</span></span>让我实在别扭<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>叶有钱嘱咐了叶轻舟点事后<span><span>，</span></span>一脸客气地对我说<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我这边也没什么事了<span><span>，</span></span>何小姐要是也没什么事的话我就先走了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我一听也是一愣<span><span>，</span></span>这个叶有钱也太客气了吧<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>我赶忙恭恭敬敬地回答<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>叶叔叔客气了<span><span>，</span></span>我只是一个小辈<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>可是叶有钱好像没听见我这句话一样<span><span>，</span></span>还是对我点点头<span><span>，</span></span>笑呵呵地说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何小姐<span><span>，</span></span>我就先走了<span><span>，</span></span>有事您给我打电话就行<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我看着叶有钱离去的背影<span><span>，</span></span>真的是越发奇怪了<span><span>。</span></span>叶家好歹也是这帝都一大家<span><span>，</span></span>这叶家家主也算是一家之主啊<span><span>，</span></span>对我一个小辈这么客气是什么意思<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>算了<span><span>，</span></span>我想不通<span><span>，</span></span>也不想了<span><span>。</span></span>我安排好了合作的事情<span><span>，</span></span>对叶轻舟说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>轻舟好久没来找我玩了<span><span>，</span></span>我都感觉身边无趣了<span><span>，</span></span>走<span><span>，</span></span>去我办公室<span><span>，</span></span>我们好好聊聊<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我拉着叶轻舟回了办公室<span><span>，</span></span>刚坐下<span><span>，</span></span>果然<span><span>，</span></span>我还没开口<span><span>，</span></span>叶轻舟就先着急忙慌地问了<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>你没事了吧<span><span>？</span></span>我看你今天气色不错的<span><span>，</span></span>你这几天休息还好吧<span><span>？</span></span>用不用我让我哥从部队医院给你调几个医生过来啊<span><span>？</span></span>我跟你说<span><span>，</span></span>我哥他们军区的医院医生水平都可高了呢<span><span>，</span></span>我给你调几个过来吧<span><span>？</span></span>平时养养也好啊……<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我接过小秘为叶轻舟准备的果汁<span><span>，</span></span>放在叶轻舟手里<span><span>，</span></span>说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>先谢谢轻舟了<span><span>，</span></span>但是你问我这么多问题我怎么可能一次性回答完呢<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何茵姐……我……我不是担心你嘛<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟不好意思地低头说<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我揉了揉叶轻舟的头发<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>放心吧<span><span>，</span></span>我已经没事了<span><span>。</span></span>所以就别再担心我了<span><span>，</span></span>好好照顾好自己<span><span>，</span></span>开开心心的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>嗯嗯嗯<span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟狠狠地点了点头<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>我会的<span><span>。</span></span>我不只能照顾好我自己<span><span>，</span></span>我还能照顾好你<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说着<span><span>，</span></span>叶轻舟还拍了拍自己的胸口<span><span>，</span></span>作出保证的样子<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我真的是被逗笑了<span><span>，</span></span>这样的女孩子也太可爱了吧<span><span>！</span></span>和我家何树正配<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>但是总要进入正题<span><span>，</span></span>不能老是迂回了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>轻舟这几天没和我一起都去干了什么啊<span><span>？</span></span>跟我说说<span><span>，</span></span>让我也开心开心<span><span>，</span></span>我这几天待在公司和家里都快闷死了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我旁敲侧击地想问出来叶轻舟的行程<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哎呀<span><span>，</span></span>何茵姐你可别提了<span><span>，</span></span>我本来说要帮你调查那个黑诊所的<span><span>，</span></span>结果第一天我还没出门就被我哥拦下了<span><span>，</span></span>我哥说不让我再插手这件事了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟突然像泄了气的皮球一样<span><span>，</span></span>撅起了小嘴向我抱怨着<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我本来计划得万无一失<span><span>，</span></span>从什么地方着手之类的<span><span>，</span></span>结果全泡汤了<span><span>，</span></span>我哥的人一直都没让我离开过叶家<span><span>。</span></span>不然我也不能找我爸带我出来找借口见你啊<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我假意庆幸地说着<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>还好你哥拦住了你<span><span>，</span></span>不然你这么莽撞的去闹怎么行<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>实则内心简直遗憾得不得了<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span>这个叶万山<span><span>，</span></span>真的坏我好事<span><span>，</span></span>我还以为他点头是要帮我呢<span><span>！</span></span>合着还是我自己想多了<span><span>，</span></span>不帮忙也就算了<span><span>，</span></span>拦着叶轻舟算怎么个意思<span><span>？</span></span>破坏我的好事……</p>
 <p>正当我内心咒骂叶万山一千遍又一千遍的时候<span><span>，</span></span>我的手机响了<span><span>，</span></span>是一个陌生电话<span><span>，</span></span>我走到窗边去接<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>您好<span><span>，</span></span>请问是何茵何女士吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>对<span><span>，</span></span>是我<span><span>，</span></span>请问您是<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哦<span><span>，</span></span>您好<span><span>，</span></span>我是 xxx 律师所的律师<span><span>，</span></span>我这边接收到了一个代理案件是关于<span><span>『</span></span>祝姣的诊疗所<span><span>』</span></span>的<span><span>，</span></span>了解到您是受害人之一<span><span>，</span></span>所以想请您于本周三下午三点出庭作证<span><span>，</span></span>您看您有时间吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我一听<span><span>，</span></span>愣住了<span><span>，</span></span>叶轻舟不是被叶万山拦住了吗<span><span>？</span></span>怎么现在还有人在调查那个诊所<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何小姐<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>电话那头看我没说话提醒了我一下<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哦哦哦<span><span>，</span></span>我在<span><span>，</span></span>我刚刚在看我的日程表<span><span>，</span></span>真是不好意思<span><span>，</span></span>我周三下午在外地出差<span><span>，</span></span>可能没有时间出庭作证<span><span>。</span></span>抱歉<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哦<span><span>，</span></span>原来是这样<span><span>，</span></span>没关系的<span><span>，</span></span>打扰您了<span><span>，</span></span>何女士再见<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>嗯<span><span>，</span></span>没事的<span><span>，</span></span>再见<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我挂了电话<span><span>，</span></span>越想越疑惑<span><span>，</span></span>叶轻舟是肯定没有去调查了<span><span>，</span></span>她没必要骗我<span><span>。</span></span>而叶万山拦着自己的妹妹<span><span>，</span></span>意图很明显<span><span>，</span></span>肯定是不想叶家插手我们何家和厉绍的恩怨<span><span>，</span></span>那肯定也不会是他<span><span>，</span></span>叶万山根本没理由这么做<span><span>。</span></span>难道是何树<span><span>？</span></span>也不能啊<span><span>，</span></span>我俩最近都住一起<span><span>，</span></span>何树整天电话都不打一个的<span><span>，</span></span>难道是提前安排好了……</p>
 <p>我越想越想不明白<span><span>，</span></span>真是烦<span><span>，</span></span>我感觉我这个恶毒女配的智商越来越跟不上这个剧情的节奏了<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span>难道这整个剧情不应该是我来推动的吗<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><strong>10</strong></p>
 <p>今天又是鸡飞狗跳的一天<span><span>。</span></span>为什么<span><span>，</span></span>你别问我为什么<span><span>，</span></span>我现在想想厉绍我就头大<span><span>，</span></span>我这个恶毒女配已经混到和霸道总裁一见面就吵架的地步了……</p>
 <p>事情是这样发生的……</p>
 <p>在被何树喂胖了好几斤后<span><span>，</span></span>我决定不能再划水了<span><span>，</span></span>我要开始认真工作了<span><span>，</span></span>工作使我快<span><span>（</span></span>减<span><span>）</span></span>乐<span><span>（</span></span>肥<span><span>）</span></span><span><span>，</span></span>毕竟作为一个恶毒女配<span><span>，</span></span>我如果没有一个强大的家底是肯定无法战胜男女主的<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>所以一大早我就踩着我的女神高跟鞋来到了办公室<span><span>，</span></span>刚到公司<span><span>，</span></span>小秘一看我斗志满满<span><span>，</span></span>就给我安排了一个很棘手的合同<span><span>，</span></span>说也是一家合作了很久的公司<span><span>，</span></span>最近不知道怎么了不太积极了<span><span>，</span></span>有想换人的意思<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我一听<span><span>，</span></span>那还了得<span><span>，</span></span>马上让小秘安排约对面老总出来吃个饭<span><span>，</span></span>谈一谈<span><span>。</span></span>小秘订了五星级酒店<span><span>，</span></span>中午就和对方老总吃个饭<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>为了表现出我们何氏的诚意<span><span>，</span></span>我早早就到了酒店<span><span>，</span></span>安排好一切<span><span>，</span></span>端庄地坐在那里就等对方老总出席<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我左等右等<span><span>，</span></span>眼看没一两分钟就到十二点了<span><span>，</span></span>可对面老总还没来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我还在想<span><span>：</span></span>这也太没有时间观念了吧<span><span>！</span></span>太没有礼貌了<span><span>，</span></span>让一个女士等他<span><span>。</span></span>等会见到人要探探情况<span><span>，</span></span>要是真的这么没有时间观念<span><span>，</span></span>这么不懂礼貌<span><span>，</span></span>这个合作不进行下去也罢<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>就在这秒针刚要走向十二<span><span>，</span></span>我即将要打电话通知秘书的时候<span><span>，</span></span>门突然被人恶狠狠地从外面推开了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我看着厉绍紧皱着眉头<span><span>，</span></span>大步流星地走到席间<span><span>，</span></span>毫不客气地拉开椅子坐下<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>太没有礼貌了<span><span>！</span></span>我看着厉绍<span><span>，</span></span>毫不客气地说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>抱歉<span><span>，</span></span>今天请的不是你<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>厉绍冷哼一声<span><span>，</span></span>没理我<span><span>，</span></span>看了一眼手表<span><span>，</span></span>又抬手向门外勾了勾<span><span>，</span></span>我的小秘躬着身<span><span>，</span></span>犹犹豫豫地带着另一个人走了进来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>那个人向我点了点头<span><span>，</span></span>然后毕恭毕敬递看向厉绍<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>厉总<span><span>，</span></span>你看我这……我能坐不<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我一脸疑惑地看向小秘<span><span>。</span></span>我记得合作案上那个公司不是厉家的吧<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>小秘赶紧跑过来<span><span>，</span></span>附在我耳边小声说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何总<span><span>，</span></span>其实我也还没弄明白怎么回事<span><span>，</span></span>就是刚刚我接住了方总<span><span>，</span></span>正要往包间来<span><span>，</span></span>结果碰上了厉总<span><span>，</span></span>厉总认识我<span><span>，</span></span>我才刚打了个招呼厉总就把方总拦下来了<span><span>，</span></span>两个人还没寒暄几句<span><span>，</span></span>厉总突然就说要把方总公司买下来……<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我听到最后明白了点<span><span>，</span></span>厉绍这就是要跟我过不去啊<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>我轻轻咳了几声<span><span>，</span></span>看着厉绍说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>厉总真是豪爽啊<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>厉绍喝了口桌上的茶<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>还不是何小姐身价高<span><span>，</span></span>我出不了这么多钱何小姐都不愿意跟我吃个饭<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>厉绍摊摊手<span><span>，</span></span>摆作无所谓的样子<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不过没关系<span><span>，</span></span>我就是钱多<span><span>，</span></span>收个小公司也不打紧<span><span>。</span></span>怎么样何小姐<span><span>，</span></span>你现在再好好想想这饭到底请的是谁<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>厉总真是智商见退<span><span>，</span></span>合同都没签<span><span>，</span></span>我自然请的还是方总啊<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我冲方总笑笑<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>方总客气地点点头<span><span>，</span></span>又瞥了一眼厉绍<span><span>。</span></span>我猜他如今一定非常难做<span><span>，</span></span>何家和厉家他谁家也得罪不起<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>方总虚擦了一把冷汗<span><span>，</span></span>小声地问厉绍<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>厉总<span><span>，</span></span>要不我先走一步回去准备收购合同<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>厉绍得意地摆摆手<span><span>，</span></span>看着我却对方总说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>有劳方总了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>然后方总就像得到大赦令一样<span><span>，</span></span>冲我点点头逃一般离开了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>意料之中的事<span><span>，</span></span>方总果然还是选择了厉绍<span><span>，</span></span>谁让厉家比何家有钱有势呢<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我坐直身体<span><span>，</span></span>对厉绍说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那厉总请吧<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>厉绍摆正身体<span><span>，</span></span>看看手表<span><span>，</span></span>又对我说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不用<span><span>，</span></span>谈谈诊疗所的案子吧<span><span>！</span></span>我们速战速决<span><span>，</span></span>我知道是你安排的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>不能吧<span><span>？</span></span>我这次什么都没做<span><span>，</span></span>厉绍就猜是我<span><span>？</span></span>狗鼻子也没这么灵吧<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>呵<span><span>」</span></span><span><span>，</span></span>我也冷哼一声<span><span>，</span></span>端着身子靠在椅背上<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>什么诊疗所<span><span>？</span></span>我去过的诊疗所多了<span><span>，</span></span>厉总指的哪一家<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你做没做咱俩心知肚明<span><span>，</span></span>何茵你别跟我装蒜<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>厉绍有点不耐烦地瞥了眼墙上的表<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我时间宝贵<span><span>，</span></span>你就说你想怎么样<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>这种时候一定要打死都不承认<span><span>，</span></span>而且这个起诉真的不是我做的<span><span>，</span></span>我怎么承认<span><span>？</span></span>我都想知道是谁这么贴心<span><span>，</span></span>帮我都安排好了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>厉绍<span><span>，</span></span>你别信口开河<span><span>，</span></span>指鹿为马<span><span>，</span></span>胡说八道的<span><span>。</span></span>你这样我可以告你污蔑的<span><span>。</span></span>咱们都是有身份的人<span><span>，</span></span>别闹得那么难看<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我一摆脸<span><span>，</span></span>拿出那种<span><span>「</span></span>打死都不是我<span><span>」</span></span>的态度<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何茵你就犟吧<span><span>，</span></span>咱俩从小长到大<span><span>，</span></span>你什么脾气我还不清楚<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>厉绍应该是还有什么着急的事情<span><span>，</span></span>所以急于想从我这里得到答案<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>行<span><span>，</span></span>你不承认也没关系<span><span>，</span></span>你怎么对姣姣的<span><span>，</span></span>就别怪我怎么对何家了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我一听<span><span>，</span></span>坐不住了<span><span>，</span></span>好大的口气<span><span>，</span></span>我也不顾什么端庄大方了<span><span>，</span></span>反正也没什么外人<span><span>，</span></span>我干脆一拍桌子站了起来<span><span>，</span></span>对着厉绍吼<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>早上起来刷牙了吗<span><span>？</span></span>这么大口气<span><span>！</span></span>厉绍你也不用跟我这耍无赖<span><span>，</span></span>我何家多大我比你清楚<span><span>，</span></span>就怕你们厉家吃不下再撑死<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>厉绍一听<span><span>，</span></span>那更是坐不住<span><span>，</span></span>霸道总裁怎么能允许有人比他还霸道呢<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何茵你都做过什么咱俩心里都有数<span><span>，</span></span>这次的事早不出晚不出<span><span>，</span></span>你去了之后就出事<span><span>，</span></span>搁谁谁不怀疑你<span><span>？</span></span>至于何家……<span><span>」</span></span>厉绍顿了一下<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我上次就说了<span><span>，</span></span>你家那十几家小公司我还真没放在眼里<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我不知道厉绍这话有没有掺水<span><span>，</span></span>但是他那个语气不知道为什么让我很不安<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>但是我肯定不能示弱<span><span>，</span></span>我不能输<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我知道我之前做了很多低智商的事<span><span>，</span></span>但是这件事真的不是我安排的<span><span>，</span></span>绝对是巧合<span><span>。</span></span>我前几天还接到出庭电话呢<span><span>，</span></span>不信你去查我通话记录<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>说着我又换了个庆幸的语气<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我还想知道是谁干得这么漂亮<span><span>，</span></span>我一定买点礼物上门感谢<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>厉绍站了起来<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>真不是你<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不是<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>然后厉绍看都没看我一眼就迈开大长腿急急地朝门口走去<span><span>，</span></span>应该是有什么他必须去处理的紧急事情<span><span>，</span></span>不然也不会进门刚坐下就跟我摊牌<span><span>，</span></span>完全不像谈判该有的套路<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>厉绍走到门口<span><span>，</span></span>突然转身<span><span>，</span></span>十分认真地对我说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何茵<span><span>，</span></span>但愿这次不是你做的<span><span>，</span></span>我可以实话告诉你<span><span>，</span></span>姣姣的诊疗所关了对你一点好处都没有<span><span>。</span></span>就算不是你<span><span>，</span></span>你最好也关注着点<span><span>。</span></span>如果是你你赶紧收手<span><span>，</span></span>不然你以后肯定后悔<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>厉绍又看了一眼手表<span><span>，</span></span>拉开大门<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>真的<span><span>，</span></span>何茵<span><span>，</span></span>你自己再好好想想吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>然后厉绍就着急忙慌地跑了出去<span><span>，</span></span>没一会<span><span>，</span></span>就有一个侍从跑上来告诉我<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何总<span><span>，</span></span>厉总已经开车走了<span><span>，</span></span>菜还上吗<span><span>？</span></span>我是记您账上还是何氏的账<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>这么快<span><span>？</span></span>厉绍这个霸道总裁的架子不要了吗<span><span>？</span></span>什么事啊<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>不过闹成这样我也没心情吃饭了<span><span>，</span></span>白白浪费了一桌子菜<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>小秘<span><span>，</span></span>我没在公司这几天辛苦你了<span><span>，</span></span>菜你打包带回去吧<span><span>！</span></span>就当是犒劳你的<span><span>，</span></span>你弄好了把菜记公司账上就行<span><span>，</span></span>正好今天周三财务会过来清账的<span><span>。</span></span>就先这样吧<span><span>，</span></span>我走了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我站起来也走了出去<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我感觉我自从监狱出来后每天过得都是奇奇怪怪<span><span>、</span></span>充满问题的<span><span>。</span></span>今天<span><span>，</span></span>我又过得一头雾水<span><span>，</span></span>我和祝姣的诊疗所关系好像比我原来认为的还要复杂<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>我这个恶毒女配太难了<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><strong>11</strong></p>
 <p>后来我知道为什么那天厉绍急急忙忙地来找我非要我收手了<span><span>，</span></span>因为那天周三啊<span><span>！</span></span>周三是什么日子<span><span>，</span></span>是祝姣案子开庭的日子啊<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>但是这我真的没办法<span><span>，</span></span>毕竟真的不是我做的<span><span>，</span></span>即使我只是小小地出了点力<span><span>。</span></span>但是我现在还是想不通我和祝姣那家诊疗所是什么样千丝万缕的关系值得厉绍离开之前再三嘱咐我收手<span><span>，</span></span>还是说这只是厉绍瞎编的<span><span>？</span></span>看着不像啊也<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>不过这个事基本也就结束了<span><span>，</span></span>案件结局其实都是可以预料的<span><span>。</span></span>祝姣那可是女主<span><span>，</span></span>是带着女主光环的人<span><span>，</span></span>再加上厉家的律师的辩护<span><span>，</span></span>最后案子也就只能以证据不足停案了<span><span>。</span></span>只要这边一停案<span><span>，</span></span>以厉绍的手段<span><span>，</span></span>祝姣基本就是没什么事了<span><span>，</span></span>罚点钱重新营业都不是问题了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>虽说这件事没有掀起什么大波浪<span><span>，</span></span>不过我本来也就是想骚扰他们一下<span><span>，</span></span>毕竟目前我还做不了什么大事<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>但是监狱那件事真的是在我心里烙下了久久的印记<span><span>，</span></span>怎么都抹不去<span><span>，</span></span>不管是为了什么<span><span>，</span></span>我就是想让祝姣也进去体验体验<span><span>。</span></span>我何茵也是有家人朋友的<span><span>，</span></span>我也想让厉绍感受感受我父母朋友的心情……</p>
 <p>但是我现在还什么都做不了<span><span>，</span></span>我要让何家<span><span>，</span></span>让自己强大起来<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>（</span></span>虽然说已经很强大了吧<span><span>，</span></span>但是欲望是无止境的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>）</span></span></p>
 <p>有了这个目标我工作都有动力了<span><span>，</span></span>也不在家混吃等死了<span><span>。</span></span>而我的乖弟弟何树依旧在我家为我准备三餐<span><span>，</span></span>比小媳妇还勤快<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>自从有了动力<span><span>，</span></span>饭桌上的话题都不再轻松愉快了……</p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>姐<span><span>，</span></span>为什么只吃米啊<span><span>？</span></span>是菜不合胃口<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我突然回过神<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>姐<span><span>，</span></span>吃饭的时候要专心<span><span>，</span></span>不然……<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不然对胃不好<span><span>，</span></span>吃饭的时候就应该把全身的血液都用到胃去消化<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我接着何树的话说着<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我的好弟弟啊<span><span>，</span></span>天天说我都背会了<span><span>。</span></span>不是你吃饭就吃饭<span><span>，</span></span>老盯着我干吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>本来就是给你做的<span><span>，</span></span>你还三心二意的……<span><span>」</span></span>何树说话声音突然小了<span><span>，</span></span>嘀咕着<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>善变的女人<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我看着<span><span>「</span></span>小怨妇<span><span>」</span></span>一样的何树<span><span>，</span></span>长叹了一口气<span><span>，</span></span>说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>好好好<span><span>，</span></span>怕了怕了<span><span>，</span></span>我认输<span><span>，</span></span>我坦白<span><span>，</span></span>不然待会什么词都能形容我了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我滑开手机锁屏<span><span>，</span></span>把小秘发给我的资料给何树看<span><span>，</span></span>何树接过手机认认真真地看了起来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>愁死我了<span><span>，</span></span>为了这事何家股价都掉了零点零零一个百分点<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我又端起碗扒了两口饭<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>这边刚掉<span><span>，</span></span>那边股东就开始给我打电话<span><span>，</span></span>一个催得比一个紧<span><span>，</span></span>你说这是我一时半会就能解决的吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>小事<span><span>，</span></span>姐<span><span>，</span></span>不管怎样我相信我姐一定能搞定的<span><span>，</span></span>所以现在你还是需要好好吃饭<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>何树一转手<span><span>，</span></span>把我的手机放在了我够不着的另一边<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我叹了口气<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>得<span><span>，</span></span>白说<span><span>，</span></span>还搭一手机<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>看着我家亲爱的弟弟这样的态度<span><span>，</span></span>我也只能把股价的事情放一边<span><span>，</span></span>听亲爱的何树弟弟的话好好吃饭了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>不过不得不说<span><span>，</span></span>我们家何树的手艺真的不错<span><span>，</span></span>越做越熟练<span><span>，</span></span>越做越合我的心意<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>吃过饭<span><span>，</span></span>我就躲进书房<span><span>，</span></span>挨个给何家的股东们打电话解释解释情况<span><span>。</span></span>我也懒得开股东大会<span><span>，</span></span>谁知道那几个老狐狸聚一块指不定又商量什么呢<span><span>，</span></span>我才不会给他们名正言顺阴谋我的机会呢<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>但这电话打的也不是一帆风顺<span><span>，</span></span>这一个个平时精明得不行<span><span>，</span></span>现在开始跟我装糊涂<span><span>，</span></span>解释半天又是听不懂又是不相信的……</p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>二叔<span><span>，</span></span>没事没事<span><span>，</span></span>我再跟你解释一遍<span><span>，</span></span>咱们好好缕缕<span><span>，</span></span>是这样的……<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你别跟我说这么多<span><span>，</span></span>咱们什么关系啊<span><span>？</span></span>阿茵<span><span>，</span></span>你就告诉我<span><span>，</span></span>你准备怎么让股价回升<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>二叔<span><span>，</span></span>股价在可控制范围内波动是正常的<span><span>，</span></span>可以接受的<span><span>，</span></span>您放心<span><span>，</span></span>没两天肯定回升<span><span>，</span></span>您别担心<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哦<span><span>，</span></span>原来你没想好应对措施啊<span><span>！</span></span>何茵<span><span>，</span></span>咱们是一家人我才给你打电话的<span><span>，</span></span>不然你以为你爸爸现在能一个电话都不给你打<span><span>？</span></span>咱们何家什么情况你应该了解啊<span><span>，</span></span>那零点零零一百分点可是不少钱呢<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>当时你爸让你接手何家的时候我就跟你爸说<span><span>，</span></span>女人就是不行<span><span>，</span></span>遇到事情光会干着急<span><span>，</span></span>不是拖着就是撒手不干<span><span>，</span></span>这种打理家业的事还是要男人来<span><span>。</span></span>我哥倒好<span><span>，</span></span>看着听进去了<span><span>，</span></span>最后却收养了一个<span><span>，</span></span>可真行<span><span>，</span></span>说到底还是想交给你<span><span>，</span></span>现在好了吧……<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>是是是<span><span>，</span></span>二叔<span><span>，</span></span>二叔别激动<span><span>，</span></span>我打理何家这么多年<span><span>，</span></span>您也是看着的<span><span>，</span></span>怎么还不放心什么啊<span><span>？</span></span>相信我<span><span>，</span></span>我……<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>嘟嘟嘟……<span><span>」</span></span>那边电话挂断了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>什么人啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我强忍着怒气保持我这何家祖传端庄的气质不口吐芬芳<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>平时跟我装家庭和睦<span><span>、</span></span>兄友弟恭<span><span>，</span></span>这时候跟我闹什么啊<span><span>？</span></span>何家股价再降也没让你们家饿着啊<span><span>！</span></span>说出去都让别人笑话<span><span>，</span></span>说起来我们何家还是书香门第<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我愤愤地翻着电话簿<span><span>，</span></span>小声念叨<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>表叔……表叔……表叔号码在哪啊<span><span>？</span></span>……<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>噔噔噔……<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我知道了何树<span><span>，</span></span>别再催我了<span><span>，</span></span>你睡吧我小点声<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>姐<span><span>，</span></span>已经十一点了<span><span>，</span></span>你都打了三个小时电话了<span><span>，</span></span>休息吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>还有几个……表叔<span><span>，</span></span>表叔电话你有吗<span><span>？</span></span>今天打到小秘那了我好像没存<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>姐水放好了<span><span>，</span></span>我试了<span><span>，</span></span>水温刚好<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>好好好<span><span>，</span></span>我马上去<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我扔下电话<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>外面一堆祖宗还不够<span><span>，</span></span>家里还供着一个<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我一拉开门<span><span>，</span></span>何树就在门口<span><span>，</span></span>拿着浴袍等着我<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>看见我出来了<span><span>，</span></span>他把浴袍递给我<span><span>，</span></span>嘱咐着<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>泡一泡解乏<span><span>，</span></span>牛奶已经给你放在浴池边了<span><span>，</span></span>你房间的热气也已经开了<span><span>，</span></span>注意点<span><span>，</span></span>别在里面睡着了<span><span>，</span></span>容易感冒<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>不知道为什么<span><span>，</span></span>我听着何树的话<span><span>，</span></span>突然刚刚的烦恼一扫而空<span><span>。</span></span>果然<span><span>，</span></span>有个贴心的弟弟就是好<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我欣慰地拍着何树的肩<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>放心<span><span>，</span></span>怎么说我也比你大<span><span>。</span></span>行了<span><span>，</span></span>你也早点睡吧<span><span>，</span></span>别熬夜<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>然后我开心地拎着浴袍走向浴池<span><span>。</span></span>身后传来何树的声音<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>还有<span><span>，</span></span>别忘记吹头发<span><span>，</span></span>不然头疼<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>晓得晓得<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我还是等你洗完吧<span><span>！</span></span>你从小就不记得吹头发<span><span>，</span></span>就喜欢头发散着自然干<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>何树看着我的背影宠溺地笑了笑<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不过还好<span><span>，</span></span>我就喜欢给你吹头发<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>来到浴池<span><span>，</span></span>我小心翼翼地探脚试了试水温<span><span>。</span></span>哦嚯嚯<span><span>，</span></span>不愧是我弟弟<span><span>，</span></span>办事和我一样可靠<span><span>。</span></span>这水温<span><span>，</span></span>舒服<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我把自己埋在水里泡了一会<span><span>，</span></span>浴池里水汽氤氲<span><span>，</span></span>朦朦胧胧的让人昏昏欲睡<span><span>。</span></span>我看见池边何树准备的牛奶<span><span>，</span></span>正好打了半天电话<span><span>，</span></span>口干舌燥的<span><span>，</span></span>我端起杯子一口饮尽了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>靠在池边想着明天要去怎么解决股价<span><span>。</span></span>想着想着<span><span>，</span></span>眼皮不自觉地打架<span><span>，</span></span>而后……</p>
 <p><span><span>（</span></span>第三视角<span><span>）</span></span></p>
 <p>过了一会<span><span>，</span></span>何树轻轻地推开浴池的门<span><span>，</span></span>早有预料一样拿起旁边椅子上的浴袍<span><span>，</span></span>蹲下身看了一眼旁边空了的玻璃杯<span><span>，</span></span>又看了一眼熟睡的何茵<span><span>。</span></span>笑了笑<span><span>，</span></span>低头轻轻地吻了一下何茵的额头<span><span>，</span></span>意犹未尽却又小心翼翼<span><span>，</span></span>就像是对待什么稀世珍宝<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>姐<span><span>，</span></span>别总拿我当弟弟一样护着了<span><span>，</span></span>我也长大了<span><span>，</span></span>小时候我想要的你都给我<span><span>，</span></span>现在你想要的我都给你<span><span>，</span></span>换我保护你<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>何树用浴袍把何茵包了起来<span><span>，</span></span>抱着何茵回了卧室……</p>
 <p><strong>12</strong></p>
 <p>今天又是一个让人感觉丰<span><span>（</span></span>头<span><span>）</span></span>富<span><span>（</span></span>昏<span><span>）</span></span>多<span><span>（</span></span>脑<span><span>）</span></span>彩<span><span>（</span></span>涨<span><span>）</span></span>的一天……</p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何树<span><span>，</span></span>你说妈叫我们回去干吗啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我坐在车里仔细回想着这几天我在公司发生的事情……</p>
 <p>难道是公司股价的事要问罪我<span><span>？</span></span>可是听那位太后娘娘跟何树电话时的语气不像啊<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>不会是真的想我了吧<span><span>？</span></span>不能啊<span><span>，</span></span>我这刚搬出来没几天啊<span><span>，</span></span>而且我天天跟她视频电话<span><span>，</span></span>不能啊<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>姐<span><span>，</span></span>妈说想我们了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>何树把车开进地下车库<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>到了<span><span>，</span></span>下车了姐<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我也只能边走边看了<span><span>，</span></span>那可是我妈<span><span>，</span></span>还能把我吃了不成<span><span>。</span></span>停好车我拉着何树进了何家大宅<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>刚推开门<span><span>，</span></span>我悄悄地观望了一下<span><span>。</span></span>我爸<span><span>，</span></span>正在沙发上看报纸<span><span>，</span></span>我妈和何姨在厨房<span><span>，</span></span>一切看起来很和谐温馨嘛<span><span>！</span></span>难倒真的是我想多了<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>我关好门<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>爸<span><span>，</span></span>妈<span><span>，</span></span>何姨<span><span>，</span></span>我和小树到了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>何父放下报纸<span><span>，</span></span>看了我和何树一眼<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>小树出去时间不短啊<span><span>！</span></span>想家了吧<span><span>，</span></span>要不是这次你姐出事<span><span>，</span></span>估计想你回来都不知道是哪年哪月了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>嗨呀<span><span>，</span></span>你个老头子<span><span>，</span></span>小树也大了<span><span>，</span></span>出去闯闯怎么不好了<span><span>？</span></span>总在家的话<span><span>，</span></span>人家孩子还怕你数落人家呢<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我妈端着菜从厨房走出来<span><span>，</span></span>招呼我和何树过去<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>茵茵<span><span>，</span></span>小树啊<span><span>，</span></span>快来<span><span>，</span></span>别听你爸的<span><span>，</span></span>他整天训人训习惯了<span><span>，</span></span>见到谁都想批评两句<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>好<span><span>，</span></span>妈<span><span>，</span></span>我和姐换个鞋就过去<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>何树笑呵呵地回应着<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我长舒了一口气<span><span>，</span></span>看来是没事<span><span>，</span></span>OK<span><span>，</span></span>那就是说这就是一个我妈想我了的小问题<span><span>。</span></span>警报解除<span><span>，</span></span>准备准备就可以安安心心地吃饭了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我开心地洗了手在桌子边坐好<span><span>，</span></span>我妈许久没见何树<span><span>，</span></span>拉着何树问这问那的<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>何父看了我们一眼<span><span>，</span></span>也放下报纸<span><span>，</span></span>洗过手<span><span>，</span></span>在主位上坐下了<span><span>。</span></span>但奇怪的是<span><span>，</span></span>明明今天就我们一家四口<span><span>，</span></span>菜却做了八九个<span><span>，</span></span>而且还十分丰盛<span><span>，</span></span>一点也没有家常的风格<span><span>，</span></span>就像是要有客人来一样<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>何父坐下了<span><span>，</span></span>看着何母和何树在一边东拉西扯的<span><span>，</span></span>笑着摇摇头<span><span>，</span></span>估计是忍不住了<span><span>，</span></span>终于扭过头问我<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>茵茵啊<span><span>，</span></span>最近公司怎么样啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>怎么……怎么样……<span><span>！</span></span>挺……挺好的啊<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我笑着打着哈哈<span><span>，</span></span>企图蒙混过关<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哦<span><span>，</span></span>挺好的啊<span><span>！</span></span>挺好的那是怎么个好法啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>何父笑着回应<span><span>，</span></span>但是那个语气给我一种并不好的感觉<span><span>，</span></span>我觉得我要是主动坦白应该有宽大处理的可能<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>索性我决定就实话实说了<span><span>，</span></span>搞不好我爸还能给我拿拿主意<span><span>。</span></span>而且这是我爸<span><span>，</span></span>我们是一家人<span><span>，</span></span>他知道了又能怎么样我<span><span>，</span></span>我可是他亲女儿<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我心一横<span><span>，</span></span>表面却漫不经心地说着<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>害<span><span>，</span></span>就是股价跌了百分之零点零零一<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我摊摊手<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>都是小事<span><span>，</span></span>本来爸要是不问我都没放在心上<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>何父点点头<span><span>，</span></span>又给自己倒了杯茶<span><span>，</span></span>品了品<span><span>，</span></span>一副高深莫测的样子<span><span>，</span></span>问<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>还有呢<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>还有<span><span>？</span></span>再有的我都不知道了<span><span>，</span></span>我怎么说啊<span><span>？</span></span>难道我爸已经可以预知未来了<span><span>？</span></span>人在家中坐<span><span>，</span></span>消息天上来吗<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>没有别的了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我一脸真诚<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>真的<span><span>，</span></span>爸<span><span>，</span></span>目前就这个事<span><span>，</span></span>别的方面公司都运行良好啊<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>何父摇摇头<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>股东们就没说点什么<span><span>？</span></span>尤其是你二叔<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>厉害厉害<span><span>！</span></span>不愧是我爸<span><span>，</span></span>这都知道<span><span>！</span></span>等等<span><span>，</span></span>不会是我二叔跟我爸告状了吧<span><span>？</span></span>不是说没跟我爸说的吗<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>我一脸尴尬<span><span>，</span></span>就像小秘密被揭穿了一样<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>爸<span><span>，</span></span>是不是二叔跟你告状了<span><span>？</span></span>我都说了我很快就能解决的<span><span>，</span></span>不会让他们吃亏的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>何父得意地笑了笑<span><span>，</span></span>就好像胜利的小孩一样<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>哪还需要浪费电话费啊<span><span>？</span></span>就你二叔那人我还能不了解<span><span>，</span></span>股价出了问题<span><span>，</span></span>第一个有反应的肯定是他<span><span>，</span></span>别的股东肯定也是受他教唆的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>就是<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我就好像寻到了知音一样<span><span>，</span></span>激动了起来<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>还是我爸看得明白<span><span>。</span></span>你说说这才多少<span><span>？</span></span>百分之零点零零一<span><span>，</span></span>这么点钱平常他们花出去看都不带看一眼的<span><span>，</span></span>这时候跟我斤斤计较<span><span>。</span></span>我什么办事能力这么多年大家都是看在眼里的<span><span>。</span></span>就这点小事就闹着全股东给我打电话<span><span>，</span></span>真是让外人见笑<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>好了<span><span>，</span></span>毕竟是你二叔<span><span>，</span></span>他那点小心思咱们知道就行了<span><span>。</span></span>股价跌了本来也就不好<span><span>，</span></span>你抓紧时间想办法吧<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>何父一口饮尽了茶<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>嗯<span><span>，</span></span>放心吧爸<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>那边何树和何母的谈话也差不多了<span><span>，</span></span>何父抬头看了一眼挂钟<span><span>，</span></span>扭头对何母说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>说的是几点来<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>七点<span><span>，</span></span>应该就快了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>何母也看了一眼表<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我一看这个场面<span><span>，</span></span>突然有种不祥的预感<span><span>，</span></span>我就说<span><span>，</span></span>今天肯定有事<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>果然<span><span>，</span></span>没一会<span><span>，</span></span>门铃响了<span><span>。</span></span>何姨端上来最后一盘菜后<span><span>，</span></span>去开了门<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我好奇地坐在那里<span><span>，</span></span>心里直犯嘀咕<span><span>。</span></span>今天请谁来吃饭啊<span><span>？</span></span>居然在家里<span><span>，</span></span>应该是跟爸妈关系很好的一个客人<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我又仔细听着门口的动静<span><span>，</span></span>听见门开的声音后<span><span>，</span></span>何父何母站了起来<span><span>，</span></span>笑呵呵地走向客厅准备迎接<span><span>。</span></span>我隐约听着客厅有高跟鞋和皮鞋的声音<span><span>，</span></span>应该不止一个人<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>随后<span><span>，</span></span>何姨的一句话直接让我愣在原地……</p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>厉先生<span><span>，</span></span>厉夫人<span><span>，</span></span>厉少爷请进<span><span>，</span></span>何先生和夫人<span><span>、</span></span>少爷<span><span>、</span></span>小姐已经在餐厅了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>what<span><span>？</span></span>搞什么飞机<span><span>？</span></span>我爸妈请厉绍他们家在我家吃饭<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span>不是这种大事我怎么能现在才知道的<span><span>、</span></span>呢<span><span>！</span></span>我俩这前几天才刚怼了一架<span><span>，</span></span>突然又要在各家长辈面前秀恩爱有点来不了啊<span><span>！</span></span>也不给个机会商量商量的吗<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>我就亦步亦趋地跟在何父何母身后<span><span>，</span></span>看着何母热情地抱了抱厉夫人<span><span>，</span></span>何父和厉绍的爸爸熟稔地握握手<span><span>，</span></span>就像多年没见的老朋友一样<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>两家人寒暄着走向餐厅<span><span>，</span></span>我趁大家不注意<span><span>，</span></span>悄悄地蹭到厉绍旁边<span><span>，</span></span>小声问着<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>什么情况<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>厉绍没好气地说着<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>等会告诉你<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>这一顿饭吃得我是手足无措<span><span>，</span></span>一会厉绍亲切地叫我<span><span>「</span></span>阿茵<span><span>」</span></span><span><span>，</span></span>一会又空中楼阁一样说着什么婚礼细节<span><span>，</span></span>时不时再给我夹个菜……</p>
 <p>总之这简直是我吃得最不安稳的一顿饭了<span><span>，</span></span>我完全不知道厉绍下一句要说什么<span><span>、</span></span>我要怎么去接话<span><span>。</span></span>唉<span><span>，</span></span>孩子太难了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你看<span><span>，</span></span>我就说这俩孩子是最配的吧<span><span>？</span></span>之前都是孩子们小不懂事<span><span>，</span></span>现在都知道大人的用心了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>厉夫人拉着何母的手说着<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>是啊<span><span>，</span></span>之前那件事是厉绍做得不妥当<span><span>。</span></span>阿绍<span><span>，</span></span>快向茵茵道个歉<span><span>，</span></span>再跟你何伯父<span><span>、</span></span>何伯母以及小树解释解释<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>厉先生看着厉绍<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我本以为就这样的霸道总裁人设<span><span>，</span></span>怎么也要发个脾气<span><span>，</span></span>端点架子吧<span><span>！</span></span>就算是同意道歉了<span><span>，</span></span>那也应该是十分不情愿<span><span>，</span></span>随随便便说声<span><span>「</span></span>对不起<span><span>」</span></span>就完了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>可谁知道厉绍居然一改霸道总裁的风格<span><span>，</span></span>认认真真地跟我说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>阿茵<span><span>，</span></span>之前贸然把你送进监狱<span><span>，</span></span>是我考虑不周<span><span>，</span></span>没有顾及你一个女孩子的感受<span><span>。</span></span>都是因为我当时太生气了<span><span>，</span></span>我现在真诚地向你道歉<span><span>，</span></span>对不起<span><span>，</span></span>请你原谅我<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说着厉绍还向我<span><span>、</span></span>何父<span><span>、</span></span>何母<span><span>、</span></span>何树各鞠了一躬<span><span>。</span></span>何树没什么反应<span><span>，</span></span>我爸妈倒是笑着接受了<span><span>。</span></span>但我真的是目瞪口呆<span><span>，</span></span>不知所措<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>虽然很想立刻就问厉绍<span><span>，</span></span>到底发生了什么<span><span>？</span></span>但是碍于长辈在场我还是没好意思开口<span><span>。</span></span>只得假装大度地说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我们马上就要订婚了<span><span>，</span></span>不用这么客气的<span><span>，</span></span>而且也是我先做错事的<span><span>，</span></span>没关系<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>两家长辈看我和厉绍这么<span><span>「</span></span>和谐<span><span>」</span></span>都满意地点点头<span><span>，</span></span>又开始天南海北的聊天了<span><span>。</span></span>何树今天一直都没什么反应<span><span>，</span></span>就自己吃着饭<span><span>，</span></span>也不看我<span><span>，</span></span>也不看厉绍<span><span>，</span></span>就好像刚刚发生的都和他没什么关系一样<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>终于吃完饭了<span><span>，</span></span>假借散步的名义<span><span>，</span></span>我和厉绍有了单独相处的机会<span><span>。</span></span>刚一出何家大门<span><span>，</span></span>厉绍就绷不住了<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>够了吗<span><span>？</span></span>够了就收手吧<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我就说<span><span>，</span></span>这就像狗改不了吃屎一样<span><span>，</span></span>霸道总裁怎么可能会变成温柔的人<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>到底怎么回事<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我一头雾水<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>怎么回事<span><span>？</span></span>你问我<span><span>？</span></span>我还想问你呢<span><span>！</span></span>你和叶万山什么时候搞上的<span><span>？</span></span>关系这么好<span><span>？</span></span>这种小事他都肯帮你<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>什么<span><span>？</span></span>叶万山<span><span>？</span></span>你的意思是祝姣的事跟叶万山有关<span><span>？</span></span>到底怎么回事<span><span>，</span></span>你说清楚点<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你真不知道<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>

 <p>这到底是怎么回事<span><span>？</span></span>难道说叶万山拦下了叶轻舟<span><span>，</span></span>自己做了后面的事<span><span>？</span></span>不能啊<span><span>！</span></span>我们没那么熟吧<span><span>！</span></span>就见了两次面而已……就算为叶轻舟也不至于亲自来吧<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>是这样<span><span>，</span></span>本来不是停案了嘛<span><span>，</span></span>我都和法官那边安排好了<span><span>，</span></span>交点钱事情就算了<span><span>，</span></span>本来也不是什么大事<span><span>。</span></span>可是原告那边迟迟不肯撤案<span><span>，</span></span>而且没过两天<span><span>，</span></span>法官又突然变卦<span><span>，</span></span>要重新开庭<span><span>。</span></span>我和姣姣一看事情不对<span><span>，</span></span>就托人打听了一下<span><span>，</span></span>你猜怎么着<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>

 <p>我这边好奇是小<span><span>，</span></span>可厉绍却突然气愤不已<span><span>，</span></span>声音都提高了好几个度冲我吼着<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那个叶万山非说姣姣的诊疗所接待过一个军部高官<span><span>，</span></span>之后高官出了事<span><span>，</span></span>这件事情军部也要彻查一下<span><span>，</span></span>以防有人借心理治疗窃取军部机密<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>厉绍气愤地喘着粗气<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>这明摆着不就是针对姣姣吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
