 <p><span><span>「</span></span>能有个什么关系<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>厉绍突然指着我说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>别以为我不知道开庭的证人都是你安排好的<span><span>。</span></span>跟你没关系<span><span>，</span></span>别装蒜了<span><span>。</span></span>虽然你可能没想闹这么大<span><span>，</span></span>但是证人这点我都能查到<span><span>，</span></span>叶万山不可能不知道<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>明摆着<span><span>，</span></span>叶万山是冲着姣姣去的<span><span>，</span></span>至于为什么……<span><span>」</span></span>厉绍瞥了我一眼<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我告诉你<span><span>，</span></span>我厉绍不是怕军部<span><span>，</span></span>怕他叶万山<span><span>，</span></span>我们厉家在京城这么多年了<span><span>，</span></span>政界<span><span>、</span></span>军部多多少少都有点人<span><span>。</span></span>我就是想这件事最后还是不要闹大<span><span>，</span></span>牵扯到姣姣的名声就不好了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说着厉绍的态度有点软了下来<span><span>，</span></span>看着我<span><span>，</span></span>说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何茵<span><span>，</span></span>两家饭也吃了<span><span>，</span></span>订婚事宜也敲定了<span><span>，</span></span>我也诚恳地道过谦了<span><span>。</span></span>叶万山那边你让他收手吧<span><span>，</span></span>别真的闹大了<span><span>，</span></span>到时候厉叶两家<span><span>，</span></span>包括你们何家都不好看<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我听着厉绍的话点了点头<span><span>，</span></span>我也觉得这件事有点出乎我的意料了<span><span>，</span></span>我确实没想闹这么大<span><span>。</span></span>现在军部都牵扯上了<span><span>，</span></span>闹大了确实不好收场了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>可是……我皱了皱眉<span><span>，</span></span>有点疑惑地说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>可是<span><span>，</span></span>我真的跟叶万山不太熟啊<span><span>！</span></span>我们总共就见过两次<span><span>，</span></span>我不知道他这么做是不是真的因为我<span><span>，</span></span>万一不是<span><span>，</span></span>那就算我去说也没有用啊<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>这不是明摆着的吗<span><span>？</span></span>没事<span><span>，</span></span>你尽管去说<span><span>，</span></span>肯定管用<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>厉绍说着<span><span>，</span></span>话风突然一转<span><span>，</span></span>有点八卦兮兮地问我<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>这叶万山一看就是喜欢你吧<span><span>，</span></span>这么说的话你应该也就不会再缠着我了吧<span><span>？</span></span>我们订婚要不要再商量商量<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>厉绍这么一说<span><span>，</span></span>我突然就像是被拔了毛的兔子<span><span>，</span></span>跳了起来<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>怎么可能<span><span>？</span></span>叶万山怎么可能喜欢我<span><span>？</span></span>我们真的就见过两面<span><span>！</span></span>估计就算跟我有关也是因为了她妹妹叶轻舟吧<span><span>，</span></span>叶轻舟倒是特别崇拜我<span><span>。</span></span>再说了<span><span>，</span></span>谁缠着你了<span><span>，</span></span>要点脸吧行吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>厉绍看我这个反应<span><span>，</span></span>也没说什么<span><span>，</span></span>摇摇头走开了<span><span>，</span></span>但还不忘提醒我<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>记得让叶万山收手<span><span>，</span></span>别忘了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>今天接收到的信息量太大了<span><span>，</span></span>送走了厉家后<span><span>，</span></span>我躺在床上拼命地回忆着我可能和叶万山有所交集的场景<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>可想来想去还是只有那两次<span><span>，</span></span>而且那两次我们也没什么交流<span><span>，</span></span>叶万山没理由喜欢我啊<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>对<span><span>，</span></span>那就一定是另一个原因——叶轻舟了<span><span>，</span></span>叶万山肯定是为了叶轻舟<span><span>。</span></span>叶轻舟跟我关系好<span><span>，</span></span>而叶轻舟被我利用去调查祝姣的诊疗所<span><span>，</span></span>叶万山不忍心自己的妹妹出面<span><span>，</span></span>就自己亲自来了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>没错<span><span>，</span></span>这样就合理了<span><span>，</span></span>一定是这样的<span><span>。</span></span>那我只要让叶轻舟跟叶万山打个招呼就行了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我想到这里<span><span>，</span></span>松了一口气<span><span>。</span></span>抓起电话就打给叶轻舟<span><span>，</span></span>想着就约她明天吃个饭<span><span>，</span></span>解释清楚<span><span>，</span></span>赶紧把厉绍和祝姣这个事情解决了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这都什么事啊<span><span>！</span></span>一步步闹得<span><span>，</span></span>真是让人头大<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><strong>13</strong></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>远远地就看见叶轻舟拎着包<span><span>，</span></span>一路小跑过来<span><span>，</span></span>然后开心地在我对面坐下<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>慢点<span><span>，</span></span>慢点<span><span>，</span></span>不着急的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我拿起果汁给叶轻舟倒了一杯<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>怎么这么开心<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>因为何茵姐约我吃饭啊<span><span>！</span></span>何茵姐想见我<span><span>，</span></span>我就开心<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟接过果汁<span><span>，</span></span>笑呵呵地看着我<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>你说一个人能活得这样单纯无忧是不是也挺好<span><span>？</span></span>叶家倒是会养女儿<span><span>，</span></span>把叶轻舟养得这么好<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>先喝点果汁<span><span>，</span></span>这是菜单<span><span>，</span></span>你看看喜欢吃什么<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我把菜单递给叶轻舟<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>好<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟也不客气<span><span>，</span></span>大大方方地接过菜单就开始点菜<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>看见叶轻舟开始点菜<span><span>，</span></span>我也就没怎么注意她了<span><span>，</span></span>一心想着我怎么组织语言才能巧妙而不漏痕迹地<span><span>，</span></span>让叶轻舟同意回去劝叶万山<span><span>，</span></span>而我却不暴露<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>我点好了<span><span>。</span></span>你今天来找我什么事啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟把菜单一合<span><span>，</span></span>递给了服务员<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>哈<span><span>？</span></span>这就完了<span><span>？</span></span>我还没点呢<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span>孩子也想吃好吃的<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span>我看着服务员离开的背影<span><span>，</span></span>算了<span><span>，</span></span>不吃就不吃吧<span><span>，</span></span>我也不差这一顿<span><span>。</span></span>有机会再教叶轻舟<span><span>，</span></span>我一定要好好强调一下这个<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>我放平心态<span><span>，</span></span>端起来我那何氏端庄优雅笑<span><span>，</span></span>说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>怎么<span><span>？</span></span>没事我就不能请你吃饭了吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>当然可以啊<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟激动地说<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我天天都想着找何茵姐你玩<span><span>，</span></span>可我哥一直都不让<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>嗯<span><span>，</span></span>那你哥呢<span><span>？</span></span>你就没问问为什么不让啊<span><span>？</span></span>我又不是什么洪水猛兽<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我旁敲侧击地打听一下叶万山的态度<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>害<span><span>，</span></span>一直都是那个借口<span><span>，</span></span>说是让你好好休息<span><span>，</span></span>不能让你操心<span><span>、</span></span>担忧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟无奈地摊摊手<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那轻舟在家有没有什么好玩的事啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我又开始了没话找话模式<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>不过叶轻舟也是孩子心性<span><span>，</span></span>一听说好玩的<span><span>，</span></span>讲起来就滔滔不绝<span><span>，</span></span>反正里面也没什么有价值的信息<span><span>。</span></span>我索性假装听着<span><span>，</span></span>再随声附和几句<span><span>，</span></span>实则还在计划怎么开口<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>还没等叶轻舟讲完<span><span>，</span></span>菜上了<span><span>，</span></span>打断了叶轻舟的话<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我笑着为叶轻舟布着菜<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>正好<span><span>，</span></span>我也饿了<span><span>，</span></span>咱们边吃边说吧<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我扫视了全桌<span><span>，</span></span>还担心没什么自己喜欢吃的菜呢<span><span>！</span></span>可没想到叶轻舟和我的口味居然差不多<span><span>，</span></span>满桌子菜基本上也都是我喜欢吃的<span><span>。</span></span>这就好了<span><span>，</span></span>起码吃的时候就不会难以下筷了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>轻舟以前来这家吃过吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我随口问了一句<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟放下筷子<span><span>，</span></span>想了想<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>没有<span><span>，</span></span>我哥管我可严了<span><span>，</span></span>基本都只让我在家吃<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哦<span><span>，</span></span>那轻舟你倒是眼光不错的<span><span>，</span></span>你点的这些啊都是这家的招牌菜呢<span><span>！</span></span>我没事来吃的时候也喜欢这些菜<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我心里已经打好草稿了<span><span>，</span></span>准备夸两句渲染一下气氛后切入正题<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>可叶轻舟接下来的话让我有点措手不及……</p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>是吗<span><span>？</span></span>那何茵姐你应该夸我哥<span><span>，</span></span>是我哥听说何茵姐你约我吃饭<span><span>，</span></span>跟我说何茵姐你喜欢这些菜的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟得意地说着<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>what<span><span>？</span></span>叶万山告诉叶轻舟我喜欢吃什么<span><span>？</span></span>这个人有读心术吗<span><span>？</span></span>还是有什么记忆宫殿看一眼就知道一个人所有喜好的那种<span><span>？</span></span>我就跟叶万山见过两次诶<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>叶轻舟的话让我把刚刚想好的措辞全都打乱了<span><span>。</span></span>我越来越好奇这个叶万山是个什么人<span><span>，</span></span>怎么好像对我特别了解一样<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我尴尬地笑了笑<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>呵呵<span><span>，</span></span>你哥知道得挺全面啊<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶轻舟听后<span><span>，</span></span>更加得意地炫耀着<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>当然啊<span><span>！</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>我哥可好了<span><span>，</span></span>他知道你很多的<span><span>。</span></span>你从小到大的经历<span><span>，</span></span>就连得过几次奖状……<span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟好像突然意识到了什么忽然闭口不说了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>我哥不是那种变态的<span><span>，</span></span>你不要多想<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟赶紧跟我解释<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>没事没事<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我假装不在意地摆摆手<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>害<span><span>，</span></span>几大家之间的竞争多激烈啊<span><span>，</span></span>攀比心作祟下了解点对手的信息很正常<span><span>，</span></span>我大学那会也看过厉绍的呢<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不是的<span><span>！</span></span>我哥从来就没想过和你竞争什么<span><span>！</span></span>我哥……我哥……他那是……他那是……<span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟情绪突然激动<span><span>，</span></span>支支吾吾纠结了起来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>他那是什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我看叶轻舟的反应<span><span>，</span></span>也好奇了起来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>叶轻舟想了想<span><span>，</span></span>鼓起勇气<span><span>，</span></span>认真地对我说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我哥那是喜欢你才去了解的<span><span>。</span></span>不是那种变态<span><span>，</span></span>更不是何茵姐你想的所谓的竞争<span><span>。</span></span>我哥是真的喜欢你<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我直接被惊呆在座位上不敢动<span><span>。</span></span>怎么<span><span>？</span></span>我和叶万山还有这种复杂美妙的关系<span><span>？</span></span>我才见他两面啊<span><span>！</span></span>这个大哥恋爱也太草率了吧<span><span>？</span></span>看着人挺稳重的啊<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哎呀<span><span>，</span></span>我又闯祸了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟自我埋怨了起来<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我感觉我哥是不想何茵姐你知道的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>说着叶轻舟拿起来电话拨了出去<span><span>，</span></span>几乎是同时那边就接通了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>喂<span><span>，</span></span>哥<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不是不是<span><span>，</span></span>不是何茵姐和我出事了<span><span>，</span></span>是……哎呀<span><span>，</span></span>是……是我一个没忍住把你喜欢何茵姐的事情说出来了<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>对不起嘛<span><span>，</span></span>我也不是故意的<span><span>，</span></span>要不你上来吧<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我就这么听着叶轻舟和叶万山的对话<span><span>，</span></span>心里宛如有一万头草泥马奔腾而过<span><span>。</span></span>这……这……这是什么狗血操作<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你哥<span><span>？</span></span>在楼下<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我试探着问<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>叶轻舟不好意思地笑了笑<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>是这样的何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>你别生气<span><span>，</span></span>我哥听说你要请我吃饭<span><span>，</span></span>他怕上次的事情再发生<span><span>，</span></span>而我一着急又没法应对才跟来的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说完<span><span>，</span></span>叶轻舟又着急地补充着<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不过我哥没进来<span><span>，</span></span>他在车里等着的<span><span>。</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>我哥真的是担心你<span><span>，</span></span>你可千万别生我哥的气<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>呵呵<span><span>，</span></span>我不生气<span><span>，</span></span>我可还是要谢谢这个大哥呢<span><span>！</span></span>都做到这种程度了<span><span>，</span></span>愿意在停车场等着保护我<span><span>，</span></span>现在就算突然说不喜欢我我也不敢信啊<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>没关系的<span><span>，</span></span>那就赶紧让叶先生上来吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我假装情绪毫无波动地平静回答<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>没事的<span><span>，</span></span>叶先生也是为我考虑<span><span>，</span></span>我怎么会生气呢<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>果然没一会<span><span>，</span></span>我就看见叶万山不紧不慢地走上来了<span><span>，</span></span>然后很礼貌地冲我笑笑<span><span>，</span></span>说着<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何小姐<span><span>，</span></span>抱歉<span><span>，</span></span>打扰了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我看着叶万山这副与我很有距离感的样子<span><span>，</span></span>哪像一个爱慕者啊<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>请坐<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶万山拉开椅子坐下了<span><span>，</span></span>叶轻舟着急地说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>哥<span><span>，</span></span>对不起嘛<span><span>，</span></span>我暴露了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>没事<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶万山安慰地摸摸叶轻舟的头<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我就知道你装不住事的<span><span>，</span></span>吃饭吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何小姐放心<span><span>，</span></span>喜欢你呢是我自己的事情<span><span>，</span></span>如果给何小姐带来什么困扰何小姐可以告诉我<span><span>，</span></span>我会尽量克制自己想去保护你的冲动<span><span>。</span></span>我也会尽量不去打扰你的生活<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我笑了一声<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那叶先生这个暗恋可够苦的<span><span>，</span></span>默默做事不留姓名<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>倾尽所有的<span><span>，</span></span>我会满足你的愿望<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶万山看着我<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>任何愿望<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说实话<span><span>，</span></span>我真的有那么一丢丢的感动<span><span>。</span></span>你说说一个人当着你的面<span><span>，</span></span>郑重其事说<span><span>，</span></span>他会尽他所有<span><span>，</span></span>去满足你的任何愿望<span><span>，</span></span>你说说你能不感动吗<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>不能<span><span>！</span></span>不可能不感动<span><span>！</span></span>但是<span><span>，</span></span>我只有那么一丢丢的感动哦<span><span>！</span></span>真的只有那么一丢丢<span><span>，</span></span>我可是恶毒女配<span><span>，</span></span>铁石心肠的那种<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那就请叶先生收手吧<span><span>！</span></span>说实话我没想闹那么大的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我看着叶万山<span><span>，</span></span>认真地说<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>别牵扯这么大了<span><span>，</span></span>到时候闹起来<span><span>，</span></span>都不好收场<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>呵<span><span>，</span></span>厉绍倒是挺清楚根源啊<span><span>，</span></span>知道让你来找我<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶万山苦笑了一下<span><span>，</span></span>但是又盯着我说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>但这也是你想要的结果吗<span><span>？</span></span>我说了<span><span>，</span></span>我会倾尽所有去实现你的愿望的<span><span>。</span></span>我不怕不好收场<span><span>，</span></span>也不会牵扯到何家<span><span>，</span></span>我就想知道你想要的是什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我突然愣住了<span><span>，</span></span>对啊<span><span>，</span></span>我想要的是什么<span><span>？</span></span>我一开始确实是想要打击一下祝姣和厉绍<span><span>，</span></span>给他们找点麻烦<span><span>。</span></span>但是后来真的当事情闹大了之后我却又不忍心了……我……</p>
 <p>我整理了一下思绪<span><span>，</span></span>也看着叶万山<span><span>，</span></span>认真地说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>首先<span><span>，</span></span>感谢叶先生的帮助<span><span>，</span></span>其次我想好了<span><span>，</span></span>我是真的没想闹这么大<span><span>，</span></span>这件事就是当时不成熟幼稚了一下而已<span><span>，</span></span>我没有理由让叶先生为我的幼稚买单<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶万山笑了笑<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那么何小姐<span><span>，</span></span>首先<span><span>，</span></span>你不用感谢我<span><span>，</span></span>一切都是我自愿的<span><span>。</span></span>其次<span><span>，</span></span>我会如你所愿的<span><span>，</span></span>但是你永远都有理由让我为你的幼稚去奋不顾身<span><span>，</span></span>因为我喜欢你<span><span>。</span></span>最后我补充一点吧<span><span>，</span></span>你可以永远都有这么幼稚的想法<span><span>，</span></span>因为只有这样才会让我能有机会为你做点什么<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我就这么看着叶万山<span><span>，</span></span>叶万山也就这么看着我<span><span>。</span></span>我突然发现这个人和我之前那两面见过的男人不一样了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>是<span><span>，</span></span>叶万山没有像厉绍那样一眼就让人挪不开眼的容貌<span><span>，</span></span>也没有厉绍那种让人印象深刻的气质<span><span>。</span></span>他甚至只是厉绍这样霸道总裁世界里的一个路人甲<span><span>。</span></span>但是<span><span>，</span></span>路人甲也有着路人甲自己的魅力<span><span>，</span></span>有些人<span><span>，</span></span>他们独特就在于百看不腻<span><span>，</span></span>每次都给你得以惊艳的机会<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哥<span><span>，</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>你们在谈什么啊<span><span>？</span></span>我怎么听不懂<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶轻舟看我们安静了<span><span>，</span></span>才弱弱地问着<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我笑着没说话<span><span>，</span></span>叶万山偏过头回答<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>没什么<span><span>，</span></span>跟你没什么关系<span><span>，</span></span>你接着吃<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶轻舟没办法只能继续无视我们默默吃饭<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我又给自己倒了点水<span><span>，</span></span>喝了一口冷静了一下<span><span>，</span></span>说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>既然这么喜欢我<span><span>，</span></span>为什么不告诉我<span><span>？</span></span>或者说<span><span>，</span></span>为什么叶先生不追我呢<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶万山没有回答<span><span>，</span></span>我又继续说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>如果叶先生在厉绍和我订婚前就开始追我的话搞不好后面所有事都不会发生了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我顿了顿<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>说不定<span><span>，</span></span>我会被感动得同意呢<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶万山冷冷地回答<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我不需要你的同情和施舍<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>然后叶万山又想了想<span><span>，</span></span>语气都温柔了点<span><span>，</span></span>颇有点委屈的感觉<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>你要是真的不喜欢我……可以……可以不回应我的<span><span>，</span></span>没关系<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说完<span><span>，</span></span>我还没来得及回答<span><span>，</span></span>叶万山就拍了拍叶轻舟<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>差不多了<span><span>，</span></span>回家吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>然后站起来就走了<span><span>，</span></span>叶轻舟一看叶万山走了<span><span>，</span></span>赶忙站起来跟过去<span><span>，</span></span>走了两步又急急地转身跟我道别<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何茵姐<span><span>，</span></span>那我和我哥先走了<span><span>，</span></span>下次再约<span><span>。</span></span>拜拜<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我冲他们笑着点点头<span><span>，</span></span>看着叶万山和叶轻舟的背影<span><span>。</span></span>仔细想想叶万山也没什么不好的<span><span>，</span></span>虽然我感觉自己好像没那么喜欢他<span><span>，</span></span>但是如果和叶家联姻的话<span><span>，</span></span>先不说家族企业的利益合作可以更牢固<span><span>，</span></span>就是叶万山这个军部的身份想来想去也是挺有用的<span><span>。</span></span>搞不好何家跌的股价能借此涨回来<span><span>，</span></span>翻一番也不是没可能啊<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>再说了<span><span>，</span></span>叶万山那么态度明显就是喜欢我<span><span>。</span></span>不过为什么他不明说呢<span><span>？</span></span>为什么他不追我呢<span><span>？</span></span>这倒是个问题・_・<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>不过没事<span><span>，</span></span>既然叶万山喜欢我<span><span>，</span></span>那么为了何家<span><span>，</span></span>为了股价<span><span>，</span></span>我就当是叶万山害羞了<span><span>，</span></span>现在都什么时代了<span><span>，</span></span>我主动追他也不是不行啊<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>我当即打电话给我的小秘<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>喂<span><span>，</span></span>小秘吗<span><span>？</span></span>帮我查查叶家长子叶万山的信息<span><span>，</span></span>详细一点<span><span>。</span></span>还有叶万山每天上班的路线<span><span>，</span></span>根据叶万山的路线再给我重新规划一份路线告诉我的司机<span><span>。</span></span>……嗯<span><span>，</span></span>对<span><span>，</span></span>是那个在军部的叶万山<span><span>，</span></span>没错<span><span>。</span></span>好<span><span>，</span></span>那就这样<span><span>，</span></span>辛苦了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>那么追叶万山就从明天开始吧<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><strong>14</strong></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何总<span><span>，</span></span>叶万山的车就在前面<span><span>，</span></span>按照您秘书给我的路线下下个路口咱们就要拐弯了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>嗯<span><span>，</span></span>这么快啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我看看前面行驶的车<span><span>，</span></span>价位不高<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>提速靠上去<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>好的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>司机听我的话提速<span><span>，</span></span>车刚与叶万山的车平齐<span><span>，</span></span>我摇下车窗<span><span>，</span></span>若无其事地说着<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>呵<span><span>，</span></span>叶先生好巧啊<span><span>？</span></span>我们顺路啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶万山也没转头看我<span><span>，</span></span>只是很无奈地说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何小姐已经跟了我两个路口了<span><span>。</span></span>何小姐<span><span>，</span></span>其实我们不顺路吧<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>啊<span><span>？</span></span>顺路顺路<span><span>，</span></span>怎么不顺路<span><span>，</span></span>有你在的路都是我的必经之路<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶万山好像附身对他的司机说了句什么<span><span>，</span></span>然后叶万山的车速突然提快了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哎<span><span>，</span></span>你至于嘛<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我拍拍我的司机示意他追上去<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>还没追上就听手机突然响了<span><span>，</span></span>是叶万山的电话<span><span>，</span></span>我匆匆忙忙地接起来<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>阿茵<span><span>，</span></span>别闹了<span><span>，</span></span>下个路口是军事管理区<span><span>，</span></span>你的车进不来的<span><span>。</span></span>你有事就直说吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>啊<span><span>？</span></span>我秘书不是这么告诉我的啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>你不用这样的<span><span>，</span></span>有事你直说吧<span><span>。</span></span>我都会同意的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那好吧<span><span>，</span></span>我想了想<span><span>，</span></span>我觉得你还可以<span><span>，</span></span>既然你不准备主动出击<span><span>，</span></span>那就换我来追你吧<span><span>。</span></span>你晚上有空吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我感觉电话对面的叶万山突然没声了<span><span>，</span></span>停了一会<span><span>，</span></span>我又再次听见叶万山的声音<span><span>，</span></span>感觉隐隐约约有点激动<span><span>，</span></span>但是不太明显<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>没有<span><span>，</span></span>我晚上没有时间<span><span>，</span></span>何小姐<span><span>，</span></span>你该转弯了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我被叶万山一提醒<span><span>，</span></span>才注意到马上就要到叶万山说的那个军事管理区了<span><span>，</span></span>我看了看好像还真的有块这样的牌子立在路中央<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我赶紧让司机转弯<span><span>，</span></span>等我再拿起手机<span><span>，</span></span>叶万山已经挂断了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>什么人啊<span><span>？</span></span>喜欢我那我主动追还不乐意<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我把手机扔在座椅上<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>（</span></span>第三视角<span><span>）</span></span></p>
 <p>叶万山在车里盯着自己的手机<span><span>，</span></span>手机界面就停在刚刚挂断电话的界面<span><span>，</span></span>那个留着何茵电话的界面……</p>
 <p>就在车内这个小小的<span><span>、</span></span>闭塞的空间里<span><span>，</span></span>离叶万山不超过一米的司机<span><span>，</span></span>或者说连叶万山自己<span><span>，</span></span>都没有发现他的呼吸加重了些许<span><span>，</span></span>他的心跳快了那么一拍<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>为什么<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>因为这是他从来就没有预料到的事<span><span>，</span></span>从他悄悄存下何茵的手机号时<span><span>，</span></span>他就没有想过自己能鼓起勇气打过去<span><span>。</span></span>更别提现在还挂断了何茵的电话<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>叶万山闭上眼睛靠在座椅上<span><span>，</span></span>嘴角却不自觉挂上一点笑容<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>他在想<span><span>：</span></span>阿茵……阿茵说她要追我……她要追我……她追我……</p>
 <p>可是很快叶万山就又沮丧了起来<span><span>，</span></span>冷嘲了一下自己<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>追你又怎么样<span><span>？</span></span>你配吗<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>（</span></span>第一视角<span><span>）</span></span></p>
 <p>虽然被叶万山拒绝了<span><span>，</span></span>但是我何茵也不是一次小挫折就能被打败的人啊<span><span>？</span></span>不然怎么会揪着厉绍不放死缠烂打到现在呢<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>所以<span><span>，</span></span>我现在正在计划着我与叶万山巧遇的二三事<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>没关系<span><span>，</span></span>上班遇不到还有下班<span><span>，</span></span>我要亲眼看看你到底有没有空<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>时间很慢<span><span>，</span></span>一分一秒的终于到了下班的时候<span><span>。</span></span>还差一分钟<span><span>，</span></span>我就已经<span><span>「</span></span>全副武装<span><span>」</span></span><span><span>，</span></span>安排好司机准备去堵叶万山<span><span>。</span></span>这架势颇有一种抢亲的既视感<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>正当我准备拉开门冲出去的时候<span><span>，</span></span>一个电话打了进来<span><span>。</span></span>我瞥了一眼手机<span><span>，</span></span>是何树<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>喂<span><span>，</span></span>小树啊<span><span>，</span></span>什么事<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>喂<span><span>，</span></span>姐<span><span>，</span></span>今天晚上你想吃什么<span><span>？</span></span>我现在在超市正好买点<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>坏了<span><span>，</span></span>我家里还有个宝藏弟弟呢<span><span>！</span></span>这我怎么解释<span><span>？</span></span>说你姐要去堵人晚上就不回去了<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>我思索再三<span><span>，</span></span>决定实话实说……</p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哦小树啊<span><span>，</span></span>你看姐姐一忙给忘了<span><span>，</span></span>今天晚上要去谈个合作的<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>啊<span><span>？</span></span>我们何家白养了一公司的人吗<span><span>？</span></span>这种场合还要你去<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>额……<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我的天<span><span>，</span></span>我被我弟弟问住了<span><span>！</span></span>而且我感觉他说得有道理<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>所以姐晚上吃什么<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不是<span><span>，</span></span>咱家股价不是刚跌嘛<span><span>，</span></span>我想着也该到我出面挽救一下的时候了<span><span>。</span></span>他们要是真的能办好事<span><span>，</span></span>这股价能跌吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>好吧<span><span>，</span></span>那姐姐早点回来<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>一定<span><span>，</span></span>你自己在家别忘了吃饭<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我放下电话<span><span>，</span></span>有点愧疚<span><span>。</span></span>算了<span><span>，</span></span>那是我弟弟嘛<span><span>，</span></span>不能因为这个怪我<span><span>。</span></span>他肯定也希望自己姐姐找到幸福的<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我这么一想<span><span>，</span></span>豁然开朗<span><span>，</span></span>拎着我的小包冲向公司门口<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我到上午和叶万山分开的地方时<span><span>，</span></span>已经过了叶万山平常下班的时间了<span><span>。</span></span>我正懊恼这个破路的堵车<span><span>，</span></span>然后就看见一辆车开到旁边<span><span>，</span></span>一个声音在我旁边响起<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何小姐也刚下班吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我心中一阵开心席卷而过<span><span>，</span></span>nice<span><span>！</span></span>没晚没晚<span><span>！</span></span>但是表面却还要保持我这个端庄大方的样子<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>哈<span><span>？</span></span>叶先生好巧啊<span><span>？</span></span>也这个时间下班啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>不巧呢<span><span>，</span></span>我本应该是早下班的<span><span>，</span></span>是何小姐太忙了<span><span>，</span></span>下班也不准时<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶万山把车窗全部摇下来<span><span>，</span></span>看着另一辆车里的我<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>这个该死的男人……怎么可以一直盯着一个女生看呢<span><span>！</span></span>多令人害羞啊<span><span>！</span></span>嗨呀<span><span>，</span></span>我就知道<span><span>，</span></span>我这该死的无处安放的魅力啊<span><span>！</span></span>叶万山这种人也遭不住<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我得意地笑笑<span><span>，</span></span>假意高冷地偏过头<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那么叶先生<span><span>，</span></span>我早上的提议你考虑好了吗<span><span>？</span></span>现在<span><span>，</span></span>你的晚上能有时间了吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶万山笑着点点头<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>当然<span><span>，</span></span>只要你开口<span><span>，</span></span>我永远都有时间<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>下车<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我对叶万山说<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>上我的车<span><span>，</span></span>让你的司机回去<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶万山宠溺地笑笑<span><span>，</span></span>然后对司机说了什么后打开车门下了车<span><span>，</span></span>走到我座位的另一边<span><span>，</span></span>敲了敲那边的车门<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那么美丽的何小姐<span><span>，</span></span>我现在可以上您的车了吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>可以了<span><span>，</span></span>刘师傅咱们去我早上定的那个地方<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶万山拉开车门和我坐在一起<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>看来我已经被何小姐安排得明明白白了<span><span>。</span></span>何小姐早有预谋啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我得意地笑了笑<span><span>，</span></span>没说话……</p>
 <p>在餐厅坐下<span><span>，</span></span>我和叶万山一句话也没说<span><span>。</span></span>而叶万山就好像在想什么事情一样<span><span>，</span></span>我感觉应该是挺棘手的<span><span>，</span></span>使得叶万山还有点纠结<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我看这个局面也不好意思问他<span><span>，</span></span>怕打断他的思路<span><span>，</span></span>万一是什么重要的事情呢<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>饭快要吃完了<span><span>，</span></span>我还在想今天这顿饭有点失败<span><span>，</span></span>我和叶万山都没什么交流<span><span>，</span></span>都没有增进感情的机会<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>可叶万山突然开口<span><span>，</span></span>一下就把我问住了<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>阿茵<span><span>，</span></span>你真的喜欢我吗<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>这真的是个送命题<span><span>，</span></span>我要是实话实说说我没那么喜欢你<span><span>，</span></span>那以后估计没有机会见面了<span><span>；</span></span>可我要是说我喜欢他<span><span>，</span></span>搞不好叶万山就会当真<span><span>，</span></span>但是我又确实没那么喜欢<span><span>，</span></span>万一被叶万山发现了那更没机会了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我太难了<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>我大脑飞快地转了一下<span><span>，</span></span>看来不能正面回答了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我笑了笑<span><span>，</span></span>凑近叶万山的耳旁小声地说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我哪里是喜欢你啊<span><span>，</span></span>我这是馋你的身子<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>这样既避开了问题<span><span>，</span></span>又活跃了我和叶万山这一晚上吃饭没说话的尴尬气氛<span><span>，</span></span>我真的是个天才<span><span>！</span></span>看来电视剧多看点也没什么坏处<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>正当我因为这个两全其美的答案沾沾自喜<span><span>，</span></span>准备坐回去的时候<span><span>，</span></span>叶万山突然伸手钳住了我的下巴<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>他叹了口气<span><span>，</span></span>摇摇头<span><span>，</span></span>然后十分温柔<span><span>，</span></span>对<span><span>，</span></span>就是十分温柔<span><span>，</span></span>还有点屈服的感觉<span><span>，</span></span>对我说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>荣幸之至<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>说完叶万山在我的额头留下了深深一吻<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>My princess<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我感觉今天也过得莫名其妙的<span><span>。</span></span>我的段位这么低吗<span><span>？</span></span>怎么已经连一个叶万山都撩不动了<span><span>！</span></span>他居然还能反杀我<span><span>！</span></span>我这个恶毒女配有点难啊……</p>
 <p><strong>15</strong></p>
 <p>今天是主动追叶万山的第五天<span><span>，</span></span>我这该死的甜美爱情啊<span><span>，</span></span>它真的死了<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span>我感觉我身上发生的这个剧情一点也不狗血<span><span>，</span></span>它的走向简直令我意想不到的美妙<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>喂<span><span>，</span></span>小叶叶啊<span><span>，</span></span>今天晚上你想去哪吃饭啊<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何小姐<span><span>，</span></span>哪里都可以<span><span>，</span></span>你定吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>那好吧<span><span>，</span></span>下班老地方见<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我挂断电话<span><span>，</span></span>唉<span><span>，</span></span>这甜美的爱情<span><span>，</span></span>真的是让人遭不住<span><span>，</span></span>天天晚上都有约会的我也是挺烦的<span><span>，</span></span>嗨呀<span><span>，</span></span>真烦<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>我和前几天一样<span><span>，</span></span>让司机开到我与叶万山分别的地方<span><span>。</span></span>果然<span><span>，</span></span>叶万山早就在那里等着了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>司机把车停在叶万山车的旁边<span><span>，</span></span>我熟练地打开车门<span><span>，</span></span>等待叶万山上车<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>可那边叶万山却突然换了主意<span><span>，</span></span>就好像是下了很大决心似的<span><span>，</span></span>郑重其事地对我说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>阿茵<span><span>，</span></span>上我的车吧<span><span>，</span></span>我带你去个地方<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span><span><span>！</span></span>我心中一阵狂喜<span><span>，</span></span>嗨呀<span><span>，</span></span>这死木头终于开窍了<span><span>！</span></span>这阿茵叫的我委实高兴<span><span>，</span></span>行行行<span><span>，</span></span>你说什么就是什么<span><span>，</span></span>都依你<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>但是<span><span>，</span></span>我表面当然还是那么温柔大方<span><span>、</span></span>端庄典雅地微微矜持了那么一小下下<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不好吧叶先生<span><span>，</span></span>我一个弱女子……<span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>那边叶万山人都忍不住笑了<span><span>，</span></span>半威胁半劝说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>那阿茵过来吗<span><span>？</span></span>不来我可就走了<span><span>，</span></span>咱们只能下次再约了<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我一听<span><span>，</span></span>哪能放过这个叶万山主动的好机会<span><span>！</span></span>这木头下次开窍都不知道什么时候了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>慌什么<span><span>，</span></span>都不能让我矜持一下<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我佯作愤怒地下了车<span><span>，</span></span>那边叶万山看我要下车了<span><span>，</span></span>也赶忙下车为我拉开了车门<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我冲叶万山笑了笑<span><span>，</span></span>附身要进车<span><span>，</span></span>这时叶万山突然莫名其妙地凑了过来<span><span>，</span></span>在我耳边小声地说了一句<span><span>：</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>阿茵<span><span>，</span></span>我爱你<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>然后叶万山就替我关上了车门<span><span>，</span></span>走到另一边坐下了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我的天<span><span>，</span></span>这么突然吗<span><span>？</span></span>哎哟<span><span>，</span></span>这点小情话弄得人家还怪不好意思的<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>叶万山上车后痴痴地看了我一眼<span><span>，</span></span>然后露出一种如临战场的表情<span><span>，</span></span>闭上了眼<span><span>，</span></span>把头扭了过去<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>回老宅吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>司机应声发动了车<span><span>。</span></span>我一脸震惊<span><span>，</span></span>这么突然吗<span><span>？</span></span>这是要见家长了<span><span>？</span></span>不行不行<span><span>，</span></span>我不能空手去吧<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我看了看叶万山<span><span>，</span></span>刚想问<span><span>，</span></span>却发现叶万山一点也没有高兴的样子<span><span>，</span></span>反而一脸凝重<span><span>，</span></span>有点懊悔又有点释然的表情<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我被他这样的表情给吓住了<span><span>，</span></span>也不敢问了<span><span>。</span></span>算了<span><span>，</span></span>就当提前走过场了<span><span>。</span></span>想来叶家那么大家业也不差我这点小礼物<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>车很快就驶进一个老旧的别墅区<span><span>，</span></span>我隐约记得叶家是暴发户出身<span><span>，</span></span>但是这里的别墅也太小太旧了吧<span><span>，</span></span>完全不符合叶家现在的身份地位啊<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>但是我也没敢提出自己的疑惑<span><span>，</span></span>这本来上门没带礼物也就算了<span><span>，</span></span>万一让叶万山听出来我嫌弃他家就更不好了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>车子左绕右拐后终于停了下来<span><span>，</span></span>这个小别墅就是那种很普通的小别墅<span><span>，</span></span>但是看着干干净净的<span><span>，</span></span>像是常年有人居住的样子<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>叶万山下车为我拉开了车门<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何小姐<span><span>，</span></span>到了<span><span>，</span></span>请下车吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>说着向我伸出了一只手<span><span>，</span></span>准备扶我<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我点点头<span><span>，</span></span>抓住了叶万山的手<span><span>，</span></span>下了车<span><span>。</span></span>叶万山就这么牵着我<span><span>，</span></span>有点如临大敌的感觉<span><span>，</span></span>然后又扭头看着我<span><span>，</span></span>我也看着他<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我俩就这么停了下来看着对方<span><span>，</span></span>有一会了<span><span>，</span></span>叶万山突然开口<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>何茵<span><span>，</span></span>我爱你<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我不知所措地点点头<span><span>，</span></span>说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我知道了<span><span>，</span></span>进去吧<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶万山听了之后紧紧地攥住了我的手<span><span>，</span></span>然后带着我一步一步走到了小别墅的门前<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何小姐<span><span>，</span></span>这是叶家最初的地方<span><span>，</span></span>我希望你看完以后不要后悔<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>what<span><span>？</span></span>叶万山不会是怕我嫌弃他家穷吧<span><span>？</span></span>好吧好吧<span><span>，</span></span>虽然叶家没有我们何家家大业大<span><span>，</span></span>但我看起来像是那种拜金女吗<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>你家穷没事啊<span><span>！</span></span>我家富就行了<span><span>，</span></span>实在不行姐姐也可以包养你啊<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我摇摇头<span><span>，</span></span>温声说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>不会的<span><span>，</span></span>我们家最初可能连别墅都买不起呢<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我安慰着叶万山<span><span>，</span></span>是啊<span><span>，</span></span>我家起家那会<span><span>，</span></span>都是在茅草屋里苦读十年考功名的读书人<span><span>，</span></span>吃饱饭估计都困难<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>叶万山有点失望地对我笑笑<span><span>，</span></span>没说话<span><span>，</span></span>然后缓缓地推开小别墅的大门<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>门完全打开了<span><span>，</span></span>我扫视了一下房子的客厅<span><span>，</span></span>其实装修还好啊<span><span>，</span></span>很有现代感<span><span>，</span></span>也不是很破旧的样子<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>我和轻舟从小就在这里长大<span><span>，</span></span>一直到十八岁<span><span>，</span></span>考上大学才离开<span><span>。</span></span>我们从小都是请老师来家里上课<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>叶万山说着<span><span>，</span></span>带着我走进这个小别墅<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我点点头<span><span>，</span></span>打量着别墅漫不经心地附和着<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>看来你家家庭条件挺好的啊<span><span>，</span></span>从小就请家教<span><span>，</span></span>你爸妈好爱你们<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>只有我和轻舟以及一些佣人住在这里<span><span>，</span></span>我爸妈他们在新宅子住<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>啊<span><span>？</span></span>这么可怜啊<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我不由地同情叶万山了<span><span>，</span></span>缺爱的孩子<span><span>，</span></span>怪不得那么木讷<span><span>，</span></span>没事<span><span>，</span></span>原谅你了<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>爸妈偶尔来看我们<span><span>，</span></span>一起吃顿饭<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我一副<span><span>「</span></span>母爱泛滥<span><span>」</span></span>的表情打量着叶万山<span><span>，</span></span>深情地说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>没关系<span><span>，</span></span>以后有我陪你啊<span><span>！</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>嗨呀<span><span>，</span></span>我这次终于展现了一下我的情商<span><span>，</span></span>还不算低吧<span><span>！</span></span></p>
 <p>叶万山听后一愣<span><span>，</span></span>并不是很高兴<span><span>。</span></span>我看叶万山的反应也是很疑惑<span><span>，</span></span>我说错话了<span><span>？</span></span>不能啊<span><span>！</span></span>难道叶万山带我来看他小时候生活的地方不是要跟我表白吗<span><span>？</span></span>不是要我了解他吗<span><span>？</span></span></p>
 <p>叶万山看我一脸懵逼<span><span>，</span></span>终于忍不住<span><span>，</span></span>一把拉过我上了二楼<span><span>，</span></span>轻车熟路地带我站在那些一模一样的门中的一扇门前<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>叶万山如释重负一般<span><span>，</span></span>推开了那扇门<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>到了这一步<span><span>，</span></span>我终于感觉到了叶万山的奇怪<span><span>，</span></span>他完全没有那种带爱人了解自己过去的兴奋和羞涩<span><span>。</span></span>反而他有一种莫名的释然却又夹杂着恐惧<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>我看着那个门一点一点地推开<span><span>，</span></span>里面的样子慢慢呈现在我眼前——是一个书房<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>书房的样式很老<span><span>，</span></span>中间有一个书桌<span><span>，</span></span>四面墙全是书<span><span>。</span></span>唯一不同的大概就是书桌后面那排架子上放的那些书吧<span><span>！</span></span>或者说他们不是书<span><span>，</span></span>而是一架子的文件夹<span><span>，</span></span>我隐约可以看见里面还有照片的样子<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>什么意思<span><span>？</span></span><span><span>」</span></span>我看向叶万山<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p>叶万山叹了口气<span><span>，</span></span>带我走到那个放满文件夹的架子<span><span>，</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我不想骗你<span><span>，</span></span>你可以自己看<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>我突然有种不祥的预感<span><span>，</span></span>我笑着看着叶万山<span><span>，</span></span>说<span><span>：</span></span><span><span>「</span></span>我都看了一天的文件了<span><span>，</span></span>没事<span><span>，</span></span>你说吧<span><span>，</span></span>我都信<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p>叶万山摇摇头<span><span>，</span></span>拉着我坐到了书桌的椅子上<span><span>，</span></span>然后随便抽了一个文件夹递给我<span><span>。</span></span></p>
 <p><span><span>「</span></span>何茵<span><span>，</span></span>打开它<span><span>。</span></span><span><span>」</span></span></p>
 <p></p>
